# Surah 40 — Ghafir

## 40:1-3 — verses 1-3 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Tafsir of Surat Ghafir

It is Meccan.

Some of the salaf, among them Muhammad ibn Sirin, disliked that it be said "al-Hawamim," and held that one should say instead "Al Ha Mim."

Abdullah ibn Mas'ud said: "Al Ha Mim" are the diba (ornamented brocade) of the Qur'an.

Ibn Abbas said: Everything has a lubab (choicest core), and the lubab of the Qur'an is "Al Ha Mim," or he said: al-Hawamim.

Mis'ar ibn Kidam said: They used to be called "al-Ara'is" (the brides).

All of this was related by the great imam Abu Ubayd al-Qasim ibn Sallam, may God have mercy on him, in his book "Fada'il al-Qur'an." Humayd ibn Zanjawayh said: [chain] Ubaydullah said: The likeness of the Qur'an is that of a man who set out to seek a dwelling place for his family, and passed by the trace of rain. While he was traveling through it, marveling at it, he came down upon soft, gentle meadows, and said: I marveled at the first rain, but this is more and more wondrous still. It was said to him: The likeness of the first rain is the likeness of the greatness of the Qur'an as a whole, and the likeness of these soft meadows is the likeness of "Al Ha Mim" within the Qur'an. Al-Baghawi related this.

Ibn Lahi'ah reported from Yazid ibn Abi Habib, that al-Jarrah ibn Abi al-Jirah told him, from Ibn Abbas, who said: Everything has a lubab, and the lubab of the Qur'an is al-Hawamim.

Ibn Mas'ud said: When I enter into "Al Ha Mim," I have entered into meadows in which I wander delightedly.

Abu Ubayd said: [chain] a man saw Abu al-Darda, may God be pleased with him, building a mosque, and said to him: What is this? He said: I am building it for the sake of "Al Ha Mim."

This mosque that Abu al-Darda built may be the mosque attributed to him inside the citadel of Damascus. Its preservation and safekeeping may be due to his blessing and the blessing of that for which it was built, for this saying indicates victory over enemies, as the Messenger of God ﷺ said to his companions during one of the military expeditions: "If you raid by night, then say: Ha Mim, they will not be granted victory," and in another narration: "you will not be granted victory."

The hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar said: [chain] from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Whoever recites Ayat al-Kursi and the beginning of Ha Mim al-Mu'min (the believer) will be protected that day from every evil."

Then he said: We do not know it to be narrated except through this chain. Al-Tirmidhi also related it from the hadith of al-Mulayki, and said: Some of the people of knowledge have criticized him regarding his memory.

In the name of God, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful

As for the discussion of the disconnected letters, it has already preceded at the beginning of Surat al-Baqarah in a manner sufficient, so there is no need to repeat it here.

It has been said that {Ha Mim} is one of the names of God, Mighty and Majestic, and they cited as evidence for this the verse:

"It reminds me of Ha Mim while the spear pierces through, so why did he not recite Ha Mim before advancing..."

It has come in the hadith related by Abu Dawud and al-Tirmidhi, from the hadith of al-Thawri, from Abu Ishaq, from al-Muhallab ibn Abi Sufrah, who said: Someone who heard the Messenger of God ﷺ told me that he said: "If you raid tonight, then say: Ha Mim, they will not be granted victory." This is a sound chain.

Abu Ubayd preferred the narration: "so say: Ha Mim, they will not be victorious," meaning: if you say that, they will not be granted victory, making it the consequence (jaza) of the command "say."

His saying, {The revelation of the Book is from God, the Almighty, the All-Knowing}, means: the revelation of this Book, which is the Qur'an, is from God, possessor of might and knowledge. His court cannot be aspired to or approached with impunity, and the smallest speck of dust is not hidden from Him even were His veil to grow thick.

His saying, {Forgiver of sin and Acceptor of repentance}, means: He forgives sin that has passed and accepts repentance in the future from whoever repents to Him and submits humbly before Him.

His saying, {severe in punishment}, means: for whoever rebels, transgresses, prefers the life of this world, is arrogant toward the commands of God, and oppresses. In this verse both hope and fear are combined together. This is like His saying, Exalted is He: {Inform My servants that I am indeed the Forgiving, the Merciful, and that My punishment is indeed the painful punishment} [al-Hijr: 49-50]. He frequently pairs these two descriptions in numerous places throughout the Qur'an, so that the servant remains between hope and fear.

His saying, {Possessor of bounty}, Ibn Abbas said: means vastness and richness. Mujahid and Qatadah said likewise.

Yazid ibn al-Asamm said: {Possessor of bounty} means: abundant good.

Ikrimah said: {Possessor of bounty} means: possessor of favor.

Qatadah said: it means possessor of blessings and excellences.

The meaning is: He is the one who bestows favor upon His servants, granting them abundantly of the graces and blessings that are His, blessings for which they are unable to give proper thanks even for a single one of them. {And if you were to count the favor of God, you would not be able to enumerate it. Indeed, man is truly unjust and ungrateful} [Ibrahim: 34].

His saying, {There is no god but He}, means: He has no equal in any of His attributes, so there is no god other than Him and no lord besides Him. {To Him is the final return}, meaning: the place of return and homecoming, where He will requite every doer according to his deed, {and He is swift in reckoning} [al-Ra'd: 41].

Abu Bakr ibn Ayyash said: I heard Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i say: A man came to Umar ibn al-Khattab, may God be pleased with him, and said: O Commander of the Faithful, I have killed someone, is there any repentance for me? So he recited to him {Ha Mim. The revelation of the Book is from God, the Almighty, the All-Knowing. Forgiver of sin and Acceptor of repentance, severe in punishment}, and said: Act, and do not despair.

Ibn Abi Hatim related it, the wording being his, and Ibn Jarir as well.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Yazid ibn al-Asamm said: There was a man from the people of Syria, a man of vigor and courage, who used to visit Umar ibn al-Khattab, may God be pleased with him. Umar noticed his absence and asked: What has become of so-and-so, son of so-and-so? They said: O Commander of the Faithful, he has taken persistently to drink. So Umar summoned his scribe and said: Write: "From Umar ibn al-Khattab to so-and-so, son of so-and-so, peace be upon you. Now then: I praise to you God, besides whom there is no god, Forgiver of sin and Acceptor of repentance, severe in punishment, Possessor of bounty, there is no god but He, to Him is the final return." Then he said to his companions: Pray to God for your brother, that he turn his heart back and that God accept his repentance. When Umar's letter reached the man, he began reading it over and repeating it, saying: Forgiver of sin and Acceptor of repentance, severe in punishment, He has warned me of His punishment and promised me that He will forgive me.

The hafiz Abu Nu'aym related it from the hadith of Ja'far ibn Burqan, adding: "He kept repeating it to himself, then he wept, then he gave up drink and gave it up thoroughly. When news of him reached Umar, may God be pleased with him, he said: This is how you should act. When you see your brother stumble into an error, guide him rightly and help him toward what is correct, and pray to God for him that He accept his repentance, and do not become helpers of Satan against him."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Thabit al-Bunani said: I was with Mus'ab ibn al-Zubayr in the countryside of Kufa, and I entered an enclosure to pray two rak'ahs. I began reciting {Ha Mim} al-Mu'min, until I reached {There is no god but He, to Him is the final return}, when there was a man behind me on a gray mule, wearing garments cut in the Yemeni style, who said: When you say {Forgiver of sin}, say: "O Forgiver of sin, forgive me my sin."

And when you say {and Acceptor of repentance}, say: "O Acceptor of repentance, accept my repentance." And when you say {severe in punishment}, say: "O severe in punishment, do not punish me." He said: I turned around and saw no one, so I went out to the gate and said: Did a man pass by you wearing Yemeni garments? They said: We saw no one. So they held the view that he was Ilyas (peace be upon him).

Then he related it through another chain, from Thabit, in similar wording, without mention of Ilyas in it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ غَافِرٍ 

وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ.

قَدْ كَرِهَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ، مِنْهُمْ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سِيرِينَ أَنْ يُقَالَ: "الْحَوَامِيمُ" وَإِنَّمَا يُقَالُ: "آلُ حم".

قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: "آلُ حم" دِيبَاجُ الْقُرْآنِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّ لِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ لُبَابًا ولُبَاب الْقُرْآنِ "آلُ حم"-أَوْ قَالَ: الْحَوَامِيمُ.

قَالَ مِسْعَر بْنُ كِدَام: كَانَ يُقَالُ لَهُنَّ: "الْعَرَائِسُ".

رَوَى ذَلِكَ كُلَّهُ الْإِمَامُ العَلم أَبُو عُبيد الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ سَلَّامٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِ: "فَضَائِلِ الْقُرْآنِ". وَقَالَ حُميد بْنُ زَنْجويه: حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ عَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: إِنْ مَثَلَ الْقُرْآنِ كَمَثَلِ رَجُلٍ انْطَلَقَ يَرْتَادُ لِأَهْلِهِ مَنْزِلًا فَمَرَّ بِأَثَرِ غَيْثٍ فَبَيْنَا هُوَ يَسِيرُ فِيهِ وَيَتَعَجَّبُ [مِنْهُ] ، إِذْ هَبَطَ عَلَى رَوْضَاتٍ دَمِثات فَقَالَ: عَجِبْتُ مِنَ الْغَيْثِ الْأَوَّلِ، فَهَذَا أَعْجَبُ وَأَعْجَبُ فَقِيلَ لَهُ: إِنَّ مَثَلَ الْغَيْثِ الْأَوَّلِ مَثَلُ عِظَم الْقُرْآنِ، وَإِنَّ مَثَلَ هَؤُلَاءِ الرَّوْضَاتِ الدَّمِثَاتِ، مَثَلُ آلِ حم فِي الْقُرْآنِ. أَوْرَدَهُ الْبَغَوِيُّ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ لَهِيعة عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ: أَنَّ الْجَرَّاحَ بْنَ أَبِي الْجِرَاحِ حَدَّثَهُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، قَالَ: لِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ لُبَابٌ، وَلُبَابُ الْقُرْآنِ الْحَوَامِيمُ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: إِذَا وَقعتُ فِي "آلِ حم" فَقَدْ وقعتُ فِي رَوْضَاتٍ أتأنَّق فِيهِنَّ .

وَقَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْأَشْجَعِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مِسْعر -هُوَ ابْنُ كِدَام -عَمَّنْ حَدَّثَهُ: أَنَّ رَجُلًا رَأَى أَبَا الدَّرْدَاءِ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] يَبْنِي مَسْجِدًا، فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَا هَذَا؟ فَقَالَ: أَبْنِيهِ مِنْ أَجْلِ "آلِ حم" .

وَقَدْ يَكُونُ هَذَا الْمَسْجِدُ الَّذِي بَنَاهُ أَبُو الدَّرْدَاءِ هُوَ الْمَسْجِدُ الْمَنْسُوبُ إِلَيْهِ دَاخِلَ قَلْعَةِ دِمَشْقَ. وَقَدْ يَكُونُ صِيَانَتُهَا وَحِفْظُهَا بِبِرْكَتِهِ وَبِرْكَةِ مَا وُضع لَهُ، فَإِنَّ هَذَا الْكَلَامَ يَدُلُّ عَلَى النَّصْرِ عَلَى الْأَعْدَاءِ، كَمَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِأَصْحَابِهِ فِي بَعْضِ الْغَزَوَاتِ: "إِنْ بَيّتم اللَّيْلَةَ فَقُولُوا: حم، لَا يُنْصَرُونَ" وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: "لَا تُنْصَرُونَ" .

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ الْحَكَمِ بْنِ ظَبْيان بْنِ خَلف الْمَازِنِيُّ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بن اللَّيْثِ الْهَمْدَانِيُّ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ مَسْعُودٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ أَبِي بَكْرٍ الْمَلِيكِيِّ، عَنْ زُرَارَةَ بْنِ مُصْعَبٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيرة، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ قَرَأَ آيَةَ الْكُرْسِيِّ وَأَوَّلَ حم الْمُؤْمِنِ، عُصِم ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمَ مَنْ كُلِّ سُوءٍ".

ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَا نَعْلَمُهُ يُروى إِلَّا بِهَذَا الْإِسْنَادِ. وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْمُلَيْكِيِّ، وَقَالَ: تَكَلَّمَ فِيهِ بَعْضُ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ مِنْ قِبَلِ حِفْظِهِ .

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

أَمَّا الْكَلَامُ عَلَى الْحُرُوفِ الْمُقَطَّعَةِ، فَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي أَوَّلِ "سُورَةِ الْبَقَرَةِ" بِمَا أَغْنَى عَنْ إِعَادَتِهِ هَاهُنَا.

وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّ ﴿حم﴾ اسْمٌ مِنْ أَسْمَاءِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَأَنْشَدُوا فِي ذَلِكَ 

يُذَكِّرُني حامِيمَ والرمحُ شَاجر ... فَهَلا تَلَا حَاميمَ قَبْل التَّقدُّمِ ...

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ الْمُهَلَّبِ بْنِ أَبِي صُفْرة قَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي مَنْ سَمِعَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِنْ بَيَّتم اللَّيْلَةَ فَقُولُوا: حم، لَا يُنْصَرُونَ" وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ .

وَاخْتَارَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ أَنْ يُروى: "فَقُولُوا: حم، لَا يُنْصَرُوا" أَيْ: إِنْ قُلْتُمْ ذَلِكَ لَا يُنْصَرُوا، جَعَلَهُ جَزَاءً لِقَوْلِهِ: فَقُولُوا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿تَنزيلُ الْكِتَابِ مِنَ اللَّهِ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ﴾ أَيْ: تَنْزِيلُ هَذَا الْكِتَابِ -وَهُوَ الْقُرْآنُ-مِنَ اللَّهِ ذِي الْعِزَّةِ وَالْعِلْمِ، فَلَا يُرَامُ جَنَابُهُ، وَلَا يَخْفَى عَلَيْهِ الذَّرُّ وَإِنْ تَكَاثَفَ حِجَابُهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿غَافِرِ الذَّنْبِ وَقَابِلِ التَّوْبِ﴾ أَيْ: يَغْفِرُ مَا سَلَفَ مِنَ الذَّنْبِ، وَيَقْبَلُ التَّوْبَةَ فِي الْمُسْتَقْبَلِ لِمَنْ تَابَ إِلَيْهِ وخَضَع لَدَيْهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ﴾ أَيْ: لِمَنْ تَمَرَّدَ وَطَغَى وَآثَرَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا، وَعَتَا عَنْ أَوَامِرِ اللَّهِ، وَبَغَى [وَقَدِ اجْتَمَعَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الرَّجَاءُ وَالْخَوْفُ] . وَهَذِهِ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿نَبِّئْ عِبَادِي أَنِّي أَنَا الْغَفُورُ الرَّحِيمُ وَأَنَّ عَذَابِي هُوَ الْعَذَابُ الألِيمُ﴾ [الْحِجْرِ: ٤٩،٥٠] يَقْرِنُ هَذَيْنِ الْوَصْفَيْنِ كَثِيرًا فِي مَوَاضِعَ مُتَعَدِّدَةٍ مِنَ الْقُرْآنِ؛ لِيَبْقَى الْعَبْدُ بَيْنَ الرَّجَاءِ وَالْخَوْفِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ذِي الطَّوْلِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي: السَّعَةَ وَالْغِنَى. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ يَزِيدُ بْنُ الأصم: ﴿ذِي الطَّوْلِ﴾ يعني: الخير الكثير.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: ﴿ذِي الطَّوْلِ﴾ ذِي الْمَنِّ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: [يَعْنِي] ذِي النِّعَمِ وَالْفَوَاضِلِ.

وَالْمَعْنَى: أَنَّهُ الْمُتَفَضِّلُ عَلَى عِبَادِهِ، الْمُتَطَوِّلُ عَلَيْهِمْ بِمَا هُوَ فِيهِ مِنَ الْمِنَنِ وَالْأَنْعَامِ، الَّتِي لَا يُطِيقُونَ الْقِيَامَ بِشُكْرِ وَاحِدَةٍ مِنْهَا، ﴿وَإِنْ تَعُدُّوا نِعْمَتَ اللَّهِ لَا تُحْصُوهَا [إِنَّ الإنْسَانَ لَظَلُومٌ كَفَّارٌ] ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ٣٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا نَظِيرَ لَهُ فِي جَمِيعِ صِفَاتِهِ، فَلَا إِلَهَ غَيْرَهُ، وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ ﴿إِلَيْهِ الْمَصِيرُ﴾ أَيِ: الْمَرْجِعُ وَالْمَآبُ، فَيُجَازِي كُلَّ عَامِلٍ بِعَمَلِهِ، ﴿وَهُوَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٤١] .

وَقَالَ أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا إِسْحَاقَ السَّبِيعي يَقُولُ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ إِلَى عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] فَقَالَ: يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ إِنِّي قَتَلْتُ، فَهَلْ لِي مِنْ تَوْبَةٍ؟ فَقَرَأَ عَلَيْهِ ﴿حم. تَنزيلُ الْكِتَابِ مِنَ اللَّهِ الْعَزِيزِ الْعَلِيمِ. غَافِرِ الذَّنْبِ وَقَابِلِ التَّوْبِ شَدِيدِ الْعِقَابِ﴾ وَقَالَ: اعْمَلْ وَلَا تَيْأَسْ.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ -وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ-وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ مَرْوَانَ الرِّقِّي، حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ أَيُّوبَ-أَخْبَرَنَا جَعْفَرِ بْنِ بَرْقان، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ الْأَصَمِّ قَالَ: كَانَ رَجُلٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الشَّامِ ذُو بَأْسٍ، وَكَانَ يَفِدُ إِلَى عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] ، فَفَقَدَهُ عُمَرُ فَقَالَ: مَا فَعَلَ فُلَانُ بْنُ فُلَانٍ؟ فَقَالُوا: يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، يُتَابِعُ فِي هَذَا الشَّرَابِ. قَالَ: فَدَعَا عُمَرُ كَاتِبَهُ، فَقَالَ: اكْتُبْ: "مِنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ إِلَى فُلَانِ ابْنِ فُلَانٍ، سَلَامٌ عَلَيْكَ، [أَمَّا بَعْدُ] : فَإِنِّي أَحْمَدُ إِلَيْكَ اللَّهَ الَّذِي لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، غَافِرُ الذَّنْبِ وَقَابِلُ التوب، شديد العقاب، ذي الطول، لا إله إِلَّا هُوَ إِلَيْهِ الْمَصِيرُ". ثُمَّ قَالَ لِأَصْحَابِهِ: ادْعُوَا اللَّهَ لِأَخِيكُمْ أَنْ يُقْبِل بِقَلْبِهِ، وَأَنْ يَتُوبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ . فَلَمَّا بَلَغَ الرَّجُلَ كتابُ عُمَرَ جَعْلَ يَقْرَؤُهُ وَيُرَدِّدُهُ، وَيَقُولُ: غَافِرُ الذَّنْبِ وَقَابِلُ التَّوْبِ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ، قَدْ حَذَّرَنِي عُقُوبَتَهُ وَوَعَدَنِي أَنْ يَغْفِرَ لِي.

وَرَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو نُعَيْمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ بُرْقَانَ، وَزَادَ: "فَلَمْ يَزَلْ يُرَدّدها عَلَى نَفْسِهِ، ثُمَّ بَكَى ثُمَّ نَزَعَ فَأَحْسَنَ النَّزْعَ فَلَمَّا بَلَغَ عُمَرَ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] خبرهُ قَالَ: هَكَذَا فَاصْنَعُوا، إِذَا رَأَيْتُمْ أَخَاكُمْ زَلَّ زلَّة فَسَدِّدُوهُ وَوَفِّقُوهُ، وَادْعُوا اللَّهَ لَهُ أَنْ يَتُوبَ عَلَيْهِ، وَلَا تَكُونُوا أَعْوَانًا لِلشَّيْطَانِ عَلَيْهِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ شَبَّة ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ وَاقِدٍ -أَبُو عُمَر الصَّفَّارُ-، حَدَّثَنَا ثَابِتٌ الْبُنَانِيُّ، قَالَ: كُنْتُ مَعَ مُصْعَبِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ فِي سَوَادِ الْكُوفَةِ، فَدَخَلْتُ حَائِطًا أَصَلِّي رَكْعَتَيْنِ فَافْتَتَحْتُ: ﴿حم﴾ الْمُؤْمِنِ، حَتَّى بَلَغْتُ: ﴿لَا إِلَهَ إِلا هُوَ إِلَيْهِ الْمَصِيرُ﴾ فَإِذَا رَجُلٌ خَلْفِي عَلَى بَغْلَةٍ شَهْبَاءَ عَلَيْهِ مُقَطَّعات يَمَنِيَّةٌ فَقَالَ: إِذَا قُلْتَ: ﴿غَافِرِ الذَّنْبِ﴾ فَقُلْ: "يَا غَافِرَ الذنب، اغفر لي ذنبي".

وَإِذَا قُلْتَ: ﴿وَقَابِلِ التَّوْبِ﴾ ، فَقُلْ: "يَا قَابِلَ التَّوْبِ، اقْبَلْ تَوْبَتِي". وَإِذَا قُلْتَ: ﴿شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ﴾ ، فَقُلْ: "يَا شَدِيدَ الْعِقَابِ، لَا تُعَاقِبْنِي". قَالَ: فَالْتَفَتُّ فَلَمْ أَرَ أَحَدًا، فَخَرَجْتُ إِلَى الْبَابِ فَقُلْتُ: مَرّ بِكُمْ رَجُلٌ عَلَيْهِ مُقَطَّعَاتٌ يَمَنِيَّةٌ؟ قَالُوا: مَا رَأَيْنَا أَحَدًا فَكَانُوا يُرَون أَنَّهُ إِلْيَاسُ.

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ طَرِيقٍ أُخْرَى، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، بِنَحْوِهِ. وَلَيْسَ فِيهِ ذِكْرُ إِلْيَاسَ.

---

## 40:4-6 — verses 4-6 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: none disputes and argues about the truth after it has been made clear and the proof has appeared, {except those who disbelieve}, meaning the deniers of the signs of Allah, His proofs and His demonstrations, {so let not their moving about in the land deceive you}, meaning in their wealth, its luxury and its splendor, as He said: {Let not the moving about of those who disbelieve in the land deceive you. It is a small enjoyment, then their abode is Hell, and how wretched is that resting place} [Al Imran: 196-197], and the Almighty said: {We let them enjoy a little, then We shall drive them to a severe punishment} [Luqman: 24].

Then the Almighty says, consoling His Prophet Muhammad ﷺ regarding the denial of those from his people who denied him, that he has an example in the prophets who came before him. For their peoples denied them and opposed them, and only a few among them believed in them. He says: {The people of Nuh denied before them}, and he was the first messenger whom Allah sent forbidding the worship of idols, {and the factions after them}, meaning from every nation, {and every nation intended to seize their messenger}, meaning they were determined to kill him by every possible means, and among them were those who killed their messenger, {and they disputed with falsehood in order to refute the truth by it}, meaning they schemed with specious argument in order to reject the clear and manifest truth.

Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] ... from Ibn Abbas (may Allah be pleased with him), from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Whoever supports falsehood in order to refute a truth by his falsehood, then the protection of Allah and the protection of His Messenger are cleared of him."

His saying: {so I seized them}, meaning I destroyed them for what they did of these sins and grave transgressions, {so how was My punishment}, meaning how did the news reach you of My punishment upon them and My retribution against them? It was indeed severe, painful, and agonizing.

Qatadah said: "By Allah, it was severe."

His saying: {And thus the word of your Lord was realized against those who disbelieved, that they are the companions of the Fire}, meaning just as the word of punishment was realized against those who disbelieved among the past nations, so likewise it is realized against the deniers among these people who denied you and opposed you, O Muhammad, by an even stronger and more fitting reasoning. For whoever denies you can have no reliability in believing anyone else.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: مَا يَدْفَعُ الْحَقَّ وَيُجَادِلُ فِيهِ بَعْدَ الْبَيَانِ وَظُهُورِ الْبُرْهَانِ ﴿إِلا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا﴾ أَيِ: الْجَاحِدُونَ لِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَحُجَجِهِ وَبَرَاهِينِهِ، ﴿فَلا يَغْرُرْكَ تَقَلُّبُهُمْ فِي الْبِلادِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي أَمْوَالِهِمْ وَنَعِيمِهَا وَزَهْرَتِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا يَغُرَّنَّكَ تَقَلُّبُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فِي الْبِلادِ. مَتَاعٌ قَلِيلٌ ثُمَّ مَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ وَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ: ١٩٦،١٩٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿نُمَتِّعُهُمْ قَلِيلا ثُمَّ نَضْطَرُّهُمْ إِلَى عَذَابٍ غَلِيظٍ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٢٤] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُسَلِّيًا لِنَبِيِّهِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ فِي تَكْذِيبِ مَنْ كَذَّبَهُ مِنْ قَوْمِهِ، بِأَنَّ لَهُ أُسْوَةَ مَنْ سَلَفَ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ؛ فَإِنَّهُ قَدْ كَذَّبَهُمْ أُمَمُهُمْ وَخَالَفُوهُمْ، وَمَا آمَنَ بِهِمْ مِنْهُمْ إِلَّا قَلِيلٌ ، فَقَالَ: ﴿كَذَّبَتْ قَبْلَهُمْ قَوْمُ نُوحٍ﴾ وَهُوَ أَوَّلُ رَسُولٍ بَعَثه اللَّهُ يَنْهَى عَنْ عِبَادَةِ الْأَوْثَانِ، ﴿وَالأحْزَابُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ، ﴿وَهَمَّتْ كُلُّ أُمَّةٍ بِرَسُولِهِمْ لِيَأْخُذُوهُ﴾ أَيْ: حَرَصُوا عَلَى قَتْلِهِ بِكُلِّ مُمْكِنٍ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ قَتَلَ رَسُولَهُ ، ﴿وَجَادَلُوا بِالْبَاطِلِ لِيُدْحِضُوا بِهِ الْحَقَّ﴾ أَيْ: مَاحَلُوا بِالشُّبْهَةِ لِيَرُدُّوا الْحَقَّ الْوَاضِحَ الْجَلِيَّ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ، حَدَّثَنَا عَارِمٌ أَبُو النعمان، حدثنا مُعْتَمِر ابن سُلَيْمَانَ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ أَبِي يُحَدِّثُ عَنْ حَنَش، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مِنْ أَعَانَ بَاطِلًا لِيَدْحَضَ بِبَاطِلِهِ حَقًّا، فَقَدْ بَرِئَتْ مِنْهُ ذِمَّةُ اللَّهِ وَذِمَّةُ رَسُولِهِ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَخَذْتُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَهْلَكَتْهُمْ عَلَى مَا صَنَعُوا مِنْ هَذِهِ الْآثَامِ وَالذُّنُوبِ الْعِظَامِ، ﴿فَكَيْفَ كَانَ عِقَابِ﴾ أَيْ: فَكَيْفَ بَلَغَكَ عَذَابِي لَهُمْ، وَنَكَالِي بِهِمْ؟ قَدْ كَانَ شَدِيدًا مُوجِعًا مُؤْلِمًا.

قَالَ قتادة: كان والله شديدًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ حَقَّتْ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَنَّهُمْ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا حَقَّتْ كلمةُ الْعَذَابِ عَلَى الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنَ الْأُمَمِ السَّالِفَةِ، كَذَلِكَ حَقَّتْ عَلَى الْمُكَذِّبِينَ مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوكَ وَخَالَفُوكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ بِطَرِيقِ الْأَوْلَى وَالْأَحْرَى؛ لِأَنَّ مَنْ كَذَّبَكَ فَلَا وُثُوقَ لَهُ بِتَصْدِيقِ غَيْرِكَ.

---

## 40:7-9 — verses 7-9 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about the angels brought near, from the four bearers of the Throne and those around it from the karubiyyin (cherubim), that they glorify their Lord with praise. That is, they combine tasbih (glorification), which indicates the negation of deficiencies, with tahmid (praise), which entails the affirmation of praiseworthy attributes. {And believe in Him}, meaning they are humble before Him and abased in His presence. And that they {seek forgiveness for those who believe}, meaning from the people of the earth among those who believe in the unseen. So God, glory be to Him, appointed His angels brought near to supplicate for the believers in their absence. Since this was among the natural traits of the angels, upon them be peace, they would say "amin" upon the supplication of a believer for his brother in his absence, as is established in Sahih Muslim: "When a Muslim supplicates for his brother in his absence, the angel says: Amin, and to you the same."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abdullah ibn Muhammad, that is Ibn Abi Shaybah, told us, Abdah ibn Sulayman told us, from Muhammad ibn Ishaq, from Ya'qub ibn Utbah, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas [may God be pleased with him], that the Messenger of God ﷺ confirmed Umayyah as truthful in something from his poetry. He said:

"A man and a bull beneath the foot of his right hand, and the eagle for the other, and a lion watching..."

The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "He spoke truly." Then he said:

"And the sun rises at the end of every night, red, its color turning rosy at dawn..."

"It refuses, and does not rise for us in its gentle course, except tormented or flogged..."

The Prophet ﷺ said: "He spoke truly."

This is a good chain of transmission. It indicates that the bearers of the Throne today are four, but on the Day of Resurrection they will be eight, as the Almighty said: {And the Throne of your Lord will be borne above them that Day by eight} [al-Haqqah: 17].

Here a question arises: how can what is understood from this verse and indicated by this hadith be reconciled with the hadith narrated by Abu Dawud:

[chain] Muhammad ibn al-Sabbah al-Bazzar told us, al-Walid ibn Abi Thawr told us, from Simak, from Abdullah ibn Umayrah, from al-Ahnaf ibn Qays, from al-Abbas ibn Abd al-Muttalib, who said: I was at al-Batha with a group among whom was the Messenger of God ﷺ, and a cloud passed over them. He looked at it and said: "What do you call this?" They said: "The sahab (cloud)." He said: "And the muzn?" They said: "And the muzn." He said: "And the 'anan?" They said: "And the 'anan." Abu Dawud said: I was not fully certain about the word 'anan. He said: "Do you know the distance between the heaven and the earth?" They said: "We do not know." He said: "The distance between them is either seventy one, seventy two, or seventy three years, then the heaven above that is likewise," until he counted seven heavens, "then above the seventh heaven there is a sea, between whose lowest and highest points is like the distance between one heaven and another. Then above that are eight mountain goats (aw'al), between whose hooves and knees is like the distance between one heaven and another. Then upon their backs is the Throne, between whose lowest and highest points is like the distance between one heaven and another. Then God, mighty and majestic, is above that." Then Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and Ibn Majah narrated it from the hadith of Simak ibn Harb, with this wording. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (a sound but singular report).

This indicates that the bearers of the Throne are eight, as Shahr ibn Hawshab said: The bearers of the Throne are eight, four of them say: "Glory be to You, O God, and with Your praise, to You belongs praise for Your forbearance after Your knowledge." And four say: "Glory be to You, O God, and with Your praise, to You belongs praise for Your pardon after Your power."

Therefore they say, when they seek forgiveness for those who believe: {Our Lord, You encompass all things in mercy and knowledge}, meaning: Your mercy encompasses their sins and errors, and Your knowledge encompasses all their deeds [and their words], their movements and their stillness. {So forgive those who have repented and followed Your way}, meaning: pardon the wrongdoers when they repent, turn back, abandon what they were engaged in, and follow what You commanded them of doing good deeds and abandoning wrongdoing. {And protect them from the punishment of the blazing Fire}, meaning: remove them far from the punishment of the Fire, which is the painful, agonizing punishment.

{Our Lord, and admit them into the Gardens of Eden which You have promised them, and whoever was righteous among their fathers, their spouses, and their descendants}, meaning: gather them together with those, so that their eyes may be delighted by being united in neighboring dwellings, as the Almighty said [glory be to Him]: {And those who believed and whose descendants followed them in faith, We will join with them their descendants, and We will not deprive them of anything of their deeds} [al-Tur: 21], meaning: We equalized them all in rank so that their eyes might be delighted, and We did not diminish the one of higher rank so that he would equal the one of lower rank. Rather, We raised up the one deficient in deeds and made him equal to the one of abundant deeds, as a favor and grace from Us.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: When the believer enters Paradise, he asks about his father, his son, and his brother, where are they? It is said to him: They did not reach your level in deeds. He says: I only worked for myself and for them. So they are joined with him in rank. Then Sa'id ibn Jubayr recited this verse: {Our Lord, and admit them into the Gardens of Eden which You have promised them, and whoever was righteous among their fathers, their spouses, and their descendants. Indeed You are the Mighty, the Wise}.

Mutarrif ibn Abdullah ibn al-Shikhkhir said: The most sincere advisers among God's creatures to the believers are the angels. Then he recited this verse: {Our Lord, and admit them into the Gardens of Eden which You have promised them}. And the most deceitful among God's creatures toward the believers are the devils.

As for His saying: {Indeed You are the Mighty, the Wise}, meaning: He who cannot be opposed or overcome, whatever He wills is, and whatever He does not will is not, the Wise in His words and His deeds, in His legislation and His decree.

{And protect them from evil deeds}, meaning: from committing them, or from their consequences for whoever falls into them. {And whoever You protect from evil deeds that Day}, meaning: the Day of Resurrection, {You have surely shown him mercy}, meaning: You have been gentle with him and saved him from punishment. {And that is the great triumph}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْمَلَائِكَةِ الْمُقَرَّبِينَ مِنْ حَمَلة الْعَرْشِ الْأَرْبَعَةِ، وَمَنْ حَوْلَهُ مِنَ الْكُرُوبِيِّينَ، بِأَنَّهُمْ يُسَبِّحُونَ بِحَمْدِ رَبِّهِمْ، أَيْ: يَقْرِنُونَ بَيْنَ التَّسْبِيحِ الدَّالِّ عَلَى نَفْيِ النَّقَائِصِ، وَالتَّحْمِيدِ الْمُقْتَضِي لِإِثْبَاتِ صِفَاتِ الْمَدْحِ، ﴿وَيُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ﴾ أَيْ: خَاشِعُونَ لَهُ أَذِلَّاءُ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، وَأَنَّهُمْ ﴿يَسْتَغْفِرُونَ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ مِمَّنْ آمَنَ بِالْغَيْبِ، فَقَيَّضَ اللَّهُ سُبْحَانَهُ مَلَائِكَتَهُ الْمُقَرَّبِينَ أَنْ يَدْعُوا لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِظَهْرِ الْغَيْبِ، وَلَمَّا كَانَ هَذَا مِنْ سَجَايَا الْمَلَائِكَةِ عَلَيْهِمُ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، كَانُوا يُؤمِّنون عَلَى دُعَاءِ الْمُؤْمِنِ لِأَخِيهِ بِظَهْرِ الْغَيْبِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ: "إِذَا دَعَا الْمُسْلِمُ لِأَخِيهِ بِظَهْرِ الْغَيْبِ قَالَ الْمَلَكُ: آمِينَ وَلَكَ بِمِثْلِهِ" .

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ -هُوَ ابْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ -حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدَةُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ يَعْقُوبَ بْنِ عُتْبَةَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ صَدّق أُمَيَّةَ فِي شَيْءٍ مِنْ شِعْرِهِ، فَقَالَ:

رَجُلٌ وَثَور تَحْتَ رِجْل يَمينه ... وَالنَّسْرُ للأخْرَى وَلَيْثٌ مُرْصَدُ ...

فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "صَدَقَ". فَقَالَ:

وَالشمس تَطلعُ كُلَّ آخِرِ لَيْلةٍ ... حَمْراءُ يُصْبحُ لَونُها يَتَوَرّدُ ...

تَأبَى فَما تَطلُع لَنَا فِي رِسْلها ... إِلَّا معَذّبَة وَإلا تُجْلدَ ...

فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "صَدَقَ" .

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ جَيِّدٌ: وَهُوَ يَقْتَضِي أَنَّ حَمَلَةَ الْعَرْشِ الْيَوْمَ أَرْبَعَةٌ، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمَ القيامة كانوا ثمانية، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَحْمِلُ عَرْشَ رَبِّكَ فَوْقَهُمْ يَوْمَئِذٍ ثَمَانِيَةٌ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١٧] .

وَهُنَا سُؤَالٌ وَهُوَ أَنْ يُقَالَ: مَا الْجَمْعُ بَيْنَ الْمَفْهُومِ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ، وَدَلَالَةِ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ؟ وَبَيْنَ الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الصَّبَّاحِ الْبَزَّارُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي ثَوْرٍ، عَنْ سِماك، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمِيرة ، عَنِ الْأَحْنَفِ بْنِ قيس، عن العباس بن عبد الْمُطَّلِبِ، قَالَ: كُنْتُ بِالْبَطْحَاءِ فِي عِصَابَةٍ فِيهِمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَمَرَّتْ بِهِمْ سَحَابَةٌ، فَنَظَرَ إِلَيْهَا فَقَالَ: "مَا تُسَمَّوْنَ هَذِهِ؟ " قَالُوا: السَّحَابَ. قَالَ: "وَالْمُزْنَ؟ " قَالُوا: وَالْمُزْنَ. قَالَ: "والعَنَان؟ " قَالُوا: وَالْعَنَانَ -قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: وَلَمْ أُتْقِنِ الْعَنَانَ جَيِّدًا -قَالَ: "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ بُعْدَ مَا بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ؟ " قَالُوا: لَا نَدْرِي. قَالَ: "بُعد مَا بَيْنَهُمَا إِمَّا وَاحِدَةٌ، أَوِ اثْنَتَانِ، أَوْ ثَلَاثٌ وَسَبْعُونَ سَنَةً، ثُمَّ السماء فوقها كذلك" حتى عَدّ سبع سموات "ثُمَّ فَوْقَ السَّمَاءِ السَّابِعَةِ بَحْرٌ ، بَيْنَ أَسْفَلِهِ وَأَعْلَاهُ مِثْلُ مَا بَيْنَ سَمَاءٍ إِلَى سَمَاءٍ، ثُمَّ فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ ثَمَانِيَةُ أوْعَال، بَيْنَ أَظْلَافِهِنَّ ورُكبهن مِثْلُ مَا بَيْنَ سَمَاءٍ إِلَى سَمَاءٍ، ثُمَّ عَلَى ظُهُورِهِنَّ الْعَرْشُ بَيْنَ أَسْفَلِهِ وَأَعْلَاهُ مِثْلُ مَا بَيْنَ سَمَاءٍ إِلَى سَمَاءٍ، ثُمَّ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَوْقَ ذَلِكَ" ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ سِمَاكِ بْنِ حَرْبٍ، بِهِ . وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ.

وَهَذَا يَقْتَضِي أَنَّ حَمَلَةَ الْعَرْشِ ثَمَانِيَةٌ، كَمَا قَالَ شَهْر بْنُ حَوْشَب: حَمَلَةُ الْعَرْشِ ثَمَانِيَةٌ، أَرْبَعَةٌ يَقُولُونَ: "سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ وَبِحَمْدِكَ، لَكَ الْحَمْدُ عَلَى حِلْمِكَ بَعْدَ عِلْمِكَ". وَأَرْبَعَةٌ يَقُولُونَ: "سُبْحَانَكَ اللَّهُمَّ وَبِحَمْدِكَ، لَكَ الْحَمْدُ عَلَى عَفْوِكَ بَعْدَ قُدْرَتِكَ".

وَلِهَذَا يَقُولُونَ إِذَا اسْتَغْفَرُوا لِلَّذِينِ آمَنُوا: ﴿رَبَّنَا وَسِعْتَ كُلَّ شَيْءٍ رَحْمَةً وَعِلْمًا﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ رَحْمَتَكَ تَسَع ذُنُوبَهُمْ وَخَطَايَاهُمْ، وَعِلْمُكَ مُحِيطٌ بِجَمِيعِ أَعْمَالِهِمْ [وَأَقْوَالِهِمْ] وَحَرَكَاتِهِمْ وَسَكَنَاتِهِمْ، ﴿فَاغْفِرْ لِلَّذِينَ تَابُوا وَاتَّبَعُوا سَبِيلَكَ﴾ أَيْ: فَاصْفَحْ عَنِ الْمُسِيئِينَ إِذَا تَابُوا وَأَنَابُوا وَأَقْلَعُوا عَمَّا كَانُوا فِيهِ، وَاتَّبَعُوا مَا أَمَرْتَهُمْ بِهِ، مِنْ فِعْلِ الْخَيْرَاتِ وَتَرْكِ الْمُنْكَرَاتِ، ﴿وَقِهِمْ عَذَابَ الْجَحِيمِ﴾ أَيْ: وَزَحْزِحْهُمْ عَنْ عَذَابِ الْجَحِيمِ، وَهُوَ الْعَذَابُ الْمُوجِعُ الْأَلِيمُ .

﴿رَبَّنَا وَأَدْخِلْهُمْ جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ الَّتِي وَعَدْتَهُمْ وَمَنْ صَلَحَ مِنْ آبَائِهِمْ وَأَزْوَاجِهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّاتِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: اجْمَعْ بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ، لِتَقَرَّ بِذَلِكَ أَعْيُنُهُمْ بِالِاجْتِمَاعِ فِي مَنَازِلَ مُتَجَاوِرَةٍ، كَمَا قَالَ [تَعَالَى] ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَاتَّبَعَتْهُمْ ذُرِّيَّتُهُمْ بِإِيمَانٍ أَلْحَقْنَا بِهِمْ ذُرِّيَّتَهُمْ وَمَا أَلَتْنَاهُمْ مِنْ عَمَلِهِمْ مِنْ شَيْءٍ﴾ [الطُّورِ: ٢١] أَيْ: سَاوَيْنَا بَيْنَ الْكُلِّ فِي الْمَنْزِلَةِ، لِتَقَرَّ أَعْيُنُهُمْ، وَمَا نَقَصْنَا الْعَالِيَ حَتَّى يُسَاوِيَ الدَّانِيَ، بَلْ رَفَعْنَا النَّاقِصَ فِي الْعَمَلِ ، فَسَاوَيْنَاهُ بِكَثِيرِ العمل، تفضلا منا ومنة.

قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: إِنَّ الْمُؤْمِنَ إِذَا دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ سَأَلَ عَنْ أَبِيهِ وَابْنِهِ وَأَخِيهِ، وَأَيْنَ هُمْ؟ فَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُمْ لَمْ يَبْلُغُوا طَبَقَتَكَ فِي الْعَمَلِ فَيَقُولُ: إِنِّي إِنَّمَا عَمِلْتُ لِي وَلَهُمْ. فَيُلحَقُونَ بِهِ فِي الدَّرَجَةِ، ثُمَّ تَلَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿رَبَّنَا وَأَدْخِلْهُمْ جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ الَّتِي وَعَدْتَهُمْ وَمَنْ صَلَحَ مِنْ آبَائِهِمْ وَأَزْوَاجِهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّاتِهِمْ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ﴾ .

قَالَ مُطرِّف بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الشِّخِّير: أنصحُ عبادِ اللَّهِ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ الملائكةُ، ثُمَّ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿رَبَّنَا وَأَدْخِلْهُمْ جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ الَّتِي وَعَدْتَهُمْ﴾ وأغشُّ عِبَادِ اللَّهِ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ الشياطينُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي لَا يُمَانَعُ وَلَا يُغَالَبُ، وَمَا شَاءَ كَانَ وَمَا لَمْ يَشَأْ لَمْ يَكُنْ، الْحَكِيمُ فِي أَقْوَالِكَ وَأَفْعَالِكَ، مِنْ شَرْعِكَ وَقَدَرِكَ 

﴿وَقِهِمُ السَّيِّئَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: فِعْلَهَا أَوْ وَبالها مِمَّنْ وَقَعَتْ مِنْهُ، ﴿وَمَنْ تَقِ السَّيِّئَاتِ يَوْمَئِذٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، ﴿فَقَدْ رَحِمْتَهُ﴾ أَيْ: لَطَفْتَ بِهِ وَنَجَّيْتَهُ مِنَ الْعُقُوبَةِ، ﴿وَذَلِكَ هُوَ الْفَوْزُ الْعَظِيمُ﴾ .

---

## 40:10-14 — verses 10-14 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about the disbelievers: that they will be called on the Day of Resurrection while they are in the depths of the fires, burning, and this is when they experience of God's punishment that which no one can bear. At that point they will loathe themselves and hate them with the utmost hatred, because of the evil deeds they had committed beforehand, which were the cause of their entering the Fire. Then the angels will inform them at that point with a lofty announcement, calling out to them, that God's hatred for them in the worldly life, when faith was presented to them and they disbelieved, was more severe than their hatred of themselves today, in this state.

Qatadah said concerning His statement: {The hatred of God is greater than your hatred of yourselves, when you were called to faith and you disbelieved} He says: God's hatred of the people of misguidance, when faith was presented to them in the worldly life and they abandoned it and refused to accept it, is greater than the hatred they will have for themselves when they witness God's punishment on the Day of Resurrection.

Al-Hasan al-Basri, Mujahid, al-Suddi, Dharr ibn Abdullah al-Hamdani, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and Ibn Jarir al-Tabari, may God have mercy on them, said likewise.

Regarding His statement: {They will say: Our Lord, You caused us to die twice and You gave us life twice} al-Thawri said, from Abu Ishaq, from Abu al-Ahwas, from Ibn Mas'ud (may God be pleased with him): This verse is like His statement: {How can you disbelieve in God when you were dead and He gave you life? Then He will cause you to die, then He will bring you to life, then to Him you will be returned} [al-Baqarah: 28]. Ibn Abbas, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, and Abu Malik said likewise. This is the correct view about which there is no doubt or uncertainty.

Al-Suddi said: They were made to die in the worldly life, then brought to life in their graves and addressed, then made to die again, then brought to life on the Day of Resurrection.

Ibn Zayd said: They were given life when the covenant was taken from them from the loins of Adam, then He created them in the wombs, then caused them to die, then gave them life on the Day of Resurrection.

These two views, from al-Suddi and Ibn Zayd, are weak, because according to what they said it would necessitate three instances of giving life and causing death. The correct view is that of Ibn Mas'ud, Ibn Abbas, and those who followed them. The point of all this is that the disbelievers will ask to be sent back while they are standing before God, Mighty and Majestic, in the courtyards of the Resurrection, as He says: {And if you could but see when the criminals hang their heads before their Lord, saying: Our Lord, we have seen and heard, so send us back that we may do righteous deeds, indeed we are now certain} [al-Sajdah: 12]. But they will not be answered. Then, when they see the Fire, witness it, stand before it, and look at the punishment and torment within it, they will ask to be sent back even more urgently than they asked the first time, but they will not be answered. God the Almighty says: {And if you could but see when they are made to stand before the Fire, and they say: Oh, would that we could be sent back, and we would not deny the signs of our Lord, and we would be among the believers. Rather, what they used to conceal before has become apparent to them. And even if they were sent back, they would return to what they were forbidden from, and indeed they are liars} [al-An'am: 27, 28]. Then when they enter the Fire and taste its touch, its crackling, its maces of iron, and its chains, their request to be sent back will be even more intense and greater: {And they will cry out therein: Our Lord, bring us out, we will do righteous deeds, other than what we used to do. Did We not give you life long enough that whoever would remember could have remembered in it, and the warner came to you? So taste, for the wrongdoers have no helper} [Fatir: 37], {Our Lord, bring us out of it, and if we return to disbelief, then indeed we are wrongdoers. He will say: Remain in it, despised, and do not speak to Me} [al-Mu'minun: 107, 108].

In this noble verse, they were gentle in their request, and they prefaced their words with an introduction, which is their statement: {Our Lord, You caused us to die twice and You gave us life twice}, meaning: Your power is immense, for You gave us life after we were dead, then You caused us to die, then You gave us life again, so You are capable of whatever You will. We have acknowledged our sins, and indeed we were wrongdoers to ourselves in the worldly abode. {So is there any way to get out?} meaning: will You grant us a way to be returned to the worldly abode? For You are capable of that, so that we may do other than what we used to do. And if we return to what we were in, then indeed we are wrongdoers. They will be answered: there is no way for you to return or go back to the worldly abode. Then the reason for preventing that is given, namely that your natures do not accept the truth and do not require it, but rather deny it and reject it. Therefore He, the Almighty, says: {That is because, when God alone was called upon, you disbelieved, but when partners were associated with Him, you believed}, meaning: this is how you are, and even if you were returned to the world you would remain so, as He says: {And even if they were sent back, they would return to what they were forbidden from, and indeed they are liars} [al-An'am: 28].

His statement: {So judgment belongs to God, the Most High, the Most Great} means: He is the Judge over His creation, the Just One who does no wrong, guiding whom He wills, leading astray whom He wills, showing mercy to whom He wills, and punishing whom He wills. There is no god but Him.

His statement: {He is the One who shows you His signs} means: He manifests His power to His creation through what they witness in His creation, both the upper and the lower realms, of the great signs that indicate the perfection of their Creator, their Originator, and their Maker. {And sends down for you provision from the sky}, which is the rain by which He brings forth crops and fruits, which is observable to the senses, in the variety of their colors, tastes, scents, forms, and hues, though it is a single water. By His immense power He has made these things differ. {And none remembers} meaning: takes heed and reflects upon these things, and uses them as evidence for the greatness of their Creator, {except one who turns in repentance}, that is, one who has insight and turns to God, Mighty and Majestic.

His statement: {So call upon God, being sincere to Him in religion, even though the disbelievers dislike it} means: devote worship and supplication to God alone in sincerity, and oppose the polytheists in their way and their doctrine.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abu al-Zubayr Muhammad ibn Muslim ibn Mudrik al-Makki said: Abdullah ibn al-Zubayr used to say, at the end of every prayer, when he gave the salutation: "There is no god but God, alone, without partner. His is the dominion and His is the praise, and He is capable of all things. There is no power and no strength except through God. There is no god but God, and we worship none but Him. His is the favor and His is the grace, and His is the excellent praise. There is no god but God, being sincere to Him in religion, even though the disbelievers dislike it." He said: The Messenger of God ﷺ used to proclaim God's oneness with these words at the end of every prayer.

Muslim, Abu Dawud, and al-Nasa'i narrated it through various chains, from Hisham ibn Urwah, Hajjaj ibn Abi Uthman, and Musa ibn Uqbah, all three from Abu al-Zubayr, from Abdullah ibn al-Zubayr, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ used to say at the end of prayer: "There is no god but God, alone, without partner," and he mentioned the rest of it in full.

It has been established in the Sahih, on the authority of Ibn al-Zubayr, that the Messenger of God ﷺ used to say following the obligatory prayers: "There is no god but God, alone, without partner. His is the dominion and His is the praise, and He is capable of all things. There is no power and no strength except through God. There is no god but God, and we worship none but Him. His is the favor and His is the grace, and His is the excellent praise. There is no god but God, being sincere to Him in religion, even though the disbelievers dislike it."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, reported that the Prophet ﷺ said: "Call upon God while being certain of a response, and know that God does not answer a supplication from a heart that is heedless and inattentive."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْكُفَّارِ: أَنَّهُمْ يُنَادَون يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَهُمْ فِي غَمَرات النِّيرَانِ يَتَلَظَّوْنَ، وَذَلِكَ عِنْدَمَا بَاشَرُوا مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا قِبَل لِأَحَدٍ بِهِ، فَمَقَتُوا عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَأَبْغَضُوهَا غَايَةَ الْبُغْضِ، بِسَبَبِ مَا أَسْلَفُوا مِنَ الْأَعْمَالِ السَّيِّئَةِ، الَّتِي كَانَتْ سَبَبَ دُخُولِهِمْ إِلَى النَّارِ، فَأَخْبَرَتْهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ إِخْبَارًا عَالِيًا، نَادَوْهُمْ [بِهِ] نِدَاءً بِأَنَّ مَقْتَ اللَّهِ لَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا حِينَ كَانَ يُعرض عَلَيْهِمُ الْإِيمَانُ، فَيَكْفُرُونَ، أَشَدُّ مِنْ مَقْتِكُمْ أَيُّهَا الْمُعَذَّبُونَ أَنْفُسَكُمُ الْيَوْمَ فِي هَذِهِ الْحَالَةِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَمَقْتُ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ مِنْ مَقْتِكُمْ أَنْفُسَكُمْ إِذْ تُدْعَوْنَ إِلَى الإيمَانِ فَتَكْفُرُونَ﴾ يَقُولُ: لمقتُ اللَّهِ أَهْلَ الضَّلَالَةِ حِينَ عُرض عَلَيْهِمُ الْإِيمَانُ فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَتَرَكُوهُ وَأَبَوْا أَنْ يَقْبَلُوهُ، أَكْبَرُ مِمَّا مَقَتُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ حِينَ عَايَنُوا عَذَابَ اللَّهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ .

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ وَمُجَاهِدٌ وَالسُّدِّيُّ وذَرُّ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الهَمْداني، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ الطبري، رحمهم الله.

وَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿قَالُوا رَبَّنَا أَمَتَّنَا اثْنَتَيْنِ وَأَحْيَيْتَنَا اثْنَتَيْنِ﴾ قَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ] : هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَيْفَ تَكْفُرُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَكُنْتُمْ أَمْوَاتًا فَأَحْيَاكُمْ ثُمَّ يُمِيتُكُمْ ثُمَّ يُحْيِيكُمْ ثُمَّ إِلَيْهِ تُرْجَعُونَ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٨] وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَأَبُو مَالِكٍ. وَهَذَا هُوَ الصَّوَابُ الَّذِي لَا شَكَّ فِيهِ وَلَا مِرْيَةَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: أُميتوا فِي الدُّنْيَا ثُمَّ أُحْيَوْا فِي قُبُورِهِمْ فَخُوطِبُوا، ثُمَّ أُمِيتُوا ثُمَّ أُحْيَوْا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: أُحْيَوْا حِينَ أُخِذَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمِيثَاقُ مِنْ صُلْبِ آدَمَ، ثُمَّ خَلَقَهُمْ فِي الْأَرْحَامِ ثُمَّ أَمَاتَهُمْ [ثُمَّ أَحْيَاهُمْ] يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَهَذَانَ الْقَوْلَانِ -مِنَ السُّدِّيِّ وَابْنِ زَيْدٍ-ضَعِيفَانِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ يَلْزَمُهُمَا عَلَى مَا قَالَا ثَلَاثُ إِحْيَاءَاتٍ وَإِمَاتَاتٍ. وَالصَّحِيحُ قَوْلُ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَمَنْ تَابَعَهُمَا. وَالْمَقْصُودُ مِنْ هَذَا كُلِّهِ: أَنَّ الْكُفَّارَ يَسْأَلُونَ الرَّجْعَةَ وَهُمْ وُقُوفٌ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فِي عَرَصَاتِ الْقِيَامَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَوْ تَرَى إِذِ الْمُجْرِمُونَ نَاكِسُو رُءُوسِهِمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ رَبَّنَا أَبْصَرْنَا وَسَمِعْنَا فَارْجِعْنَا نَعْمَلْ صَالِحًا إِنَّا مُوقِنُونَ﴾ [السَّجْدَةِ:١٢] ، فَلَا يُجَابُونَ. ثُمَّ إِذَا رَأَوُا النَّارَ وَعَايَنُوهَا وَوَقَفُوا عَلَيْهَا، وَنَظَرُوا إِلَى مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْعَذَابِ والنَّكال، سَأَلُوا الرَّجْعَةَ أَشَدَّ مِمَّا سَأَلُوا أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ، فَلَا يُجَابُونَ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ تَرَى إِذْ وُقِفُوا عَلَى النَّارِ فَقَالُوا يَا لَيْتَنَا نُرَدُّ وَلا نُكَذِّبَ بِآيَاتِ رَبِّنَا وَنَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ بَلْ بَدَا لَهُمْ مَا كَانُوا يُخْفُونَ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَلَوْ رُدُّوا لَعَادُوا لِمَا نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَإِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُون﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ:٢٧، ٢٨] فَإِذَا دَخَلُوا النَّارَ وَذَاقُوا مَسّها وحَسِيسها وَمَقَامِعَهَا وَأَغْلَالَهَا، كَانَ سؤُالهم لِلرَّجْعَةِ أَشَدَّ وَأَعْظَمَ، ﴿وَهُمْ يَصْطَرِخُونَ فِيهَا رَبَّنَا أَخْرِجْنَا نَعْمَلْ صَالِحًا غَيْرَ الَّذِي كُنَّا نَعْمَلُ أَوَلَمْ نُعَمِّرْكُمْ مَا يَتَذَكَّرُ فِيهِ مَنْ تَذَكَّرَ وَجَاءَكُمُ النَّذِيرُ فَذُوقُوا فَمَا لِلظَّالِمِينَ مِنْ نَصِيرٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ:٣٧] ، ﴿رَبَّنَا أَخْرِجْنَا مِنْهَا فَإِنْ عُدْنَا فَإِنَّا ظَالِمُونَ. قَالَ اخْسَئُوا فِيهَا وَلا تُكَلِّمُونِ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١٠٧، ١٠٨] ، وَفِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ تَلَطَّفُوا فِي السُّؤَالِ، وَقَدَّمُوا بَيْنَ يَدَيْ كَلَامِهِمْ مُقدّمة، وَهِيَ قَوْلُهُمْ: ﴿رَبَّنَا أَمَتَّنَا اثْنَتَيْنِ وَأَحْيَيْتَنَا اثْنَتَيْنِ﴾ أَيْ: قُدْرَتُكَ عَظِيمَةٌ، فَإِنَّكَ أَحْيَيْتَنَا بَعْدَ مَا كُنَّا أَمْوَاتًا، ثُمَّ أَمَتَّنَا ثُمَّ أَحْيَيْتَنَا، فَأَنْتَ قَادِرٌ عَلَى مَا تَشَاءُ، وَقَدِ اعْتَرَفْنَا بِذُنُوبِنَا، وَإِنَّنَا كُنَّا ظَالِمِينَ لِأَنْفُسِنَا فِي الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا، ﴿فَهَلْ إِلَى خُرُوجٍ مِنْ سَبِيلٍ﴾ أَيْ فَهَلْ أَنْتَ مُجِيبُنَا إِلَى أَنْ تُعِيدَنَا إِلَى الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا؟ فَإِنَّكَ قَادِرٌ عَلَى ذَلِكَ؛ لِنَعْمَلَ غَيْرَ الَّذِي كُنَّا نَعْمَلُ، فَإِنْ عُدْنَا إِلَى مَا كُنَّا فِيهِ فَإِنَّا ظَالِمُونَ. فأُجِيبُوا أَلَّا سَبِيلَ إِلَى عَوْدِكُمْ وَمَرْجِعِكُمْ إِلَى الدَّارِ الدُّنْيَا. ثُمَّ عَلَّلَ الْمَنْعَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ بِأَنَّ سَجَايَاكُمْ لَا تَقْبَلُ الْحَقَّ وَلَا تَقْتَضِيهِ بَلْ تَجْحَده وَتَنْفِيهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ذَلِكُمْ بِأَنَّهُ إِذَا دُعِيَ اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ كَفَرْتُمْ وَإِنْ يُشْرَكْ بِهِ تُؤْمِنُوا﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتُمْ هَكَذَا تَكُونُونَ، وَإِنْ رُدِدْتُمْ إِلَى الدُّنْيَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ رُدُّوا لَعَادُوا لِمَا نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَإِنَّهُمْ لَكَاذِبُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٢٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَالْحُكْمُ لِلَّهِ الْعَلِيِّ الْكَبِيرِ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ الْحَاكِمُ فِي خَلْقِهِ، الْعَادِلُ الَّذِي لَا يَجُورُ، فَيَهْدِي مَنْ يشاء، ويضل من يشاء، ويرحم من يشاء، وَيُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿هُوَ الَّذِي يُرِيكُمْ آيَاتِهِ﴾ أَيْ: يُظْهِرُ قُدْرَتَهُ لِخَلْقِهِ بِمَا يُشَاهِدُونَهُ فِي خَلْقِهِ الْعُلْوِيِّ وَالسُّفْلِيِّ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ الْعَظِيمَةِ الدَّالَّةِ عَلَى كَمَالِ خَالِقِهَا وَمُبْدِعِهَا وَمُنْشِئِهَا، ﴿وَيُنزلُ لَكُمْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ رِزْقًا﴾ ، وَهُوَ الْمَطَرُ الَّذِي يُخْرِجُ بِهِ مِنَ الزُّرُوعِ وَالثِّمَارِ مَا هُوَ مُشَاهَدٌ بِالْحِسِّ، مِنِ اخْتِلَافِ أَلْوَانِهِ وَطَعُومِهِ، وَرَوَائِحِهِ وَأَشْكَالِهِ وَأَلْوَانِهِ، وَهُوَ مَاءٌ وَاحِدٌ، فَبِالْقُدْرَةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ فَاوَتَ بَيْنَ هَذِهِ الْأَشْيَاءِ، ﴿وَمَا يَتَذَكَّرُ﴾ أَيْ: يَعْتَبِرُ وَيَتَفَكَّرُ فِي هَذِهِ الْأَشْيَاءِ وَيَسْتَدِلُّ بِهَا عَلَى عَظَمَةِ خَالِقِهَا ﴿إِلا مَنْ يُنِيبُ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ هُوَ بَصِيرٌ مُنِيبٌ إِلَى اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَادْعُوا اللَّهَ مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ وَلَوْ كَرِهَ الْكَافِرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَأَخْلِصُوا لِلَّهِ وَحْدَهُ الْعِبَادَةَ وَالدُّعَاءَ، وَخَالِفُوا الْمُشْرِكِينَ فِي مَسْلَكِهِمْ وَمَذْهَبِهِمْ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ نُمَيْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامٌ -يعني بن عُرْوَةَ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ-عَنْ أَبِي الزُّبَيْرِ مُحَمَّدِ بن مسلم بن مدرس الْمَكِّيِّ قَالَ: كَانَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ يَقُولُ فِي دُبُرِ كُلِّ صَلَاةٍ حِينَ يُسَلِّمُ : لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ، وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ، لَا حَوْلَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَلَا نَعْبُدُ إِلَّا إِيَّاهُ، لَهُ النِّعْمَةُ وَلَهُ الْفَضْلُ، وَلَهُ الثَّنَاءُ الْحَسَنُ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ وَلَوْ كَرِهَ الْكَافِرُونَ" قَالَ: وَكَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُهَلِّل بِهِنَّ دُبُرَ كُلِّ صَلَاةٍ .

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، وَحَجَّاجِ بْنِ أَبِي عُثْمَانَ، وَمُوسَى بْنِ عُقْبَةَ، ثَلَاثَتُهُمْ عَنْ أَبِي الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ فِي دُبُرِ الصَّلَاةِ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَهُ .

وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنِ ابْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَقُولُ عَقِبَ الصَّلَوَاتِ الْمَكْتُوبَاتِ: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ، وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ، وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ. لَا حَوْلَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ وَلَا نَعْبُدُ إِلَّا إِيَّاهُ، لَهُ النِّعْمَةُ وَلَهُ الْفَضْلُ، وَلَهُ الثَّنَاءُ الْحَسَنُ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ وَلَوْ كَرِهَ الْكَافِرُونَ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الرَّبِيعُ حَدَّثَنَا الخَصِيب بْنُ نَاصِحٍ، حَدَّثَنَا صَالِحٌ -يَعْنِي المِرِّي-عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ حَسَّانَ، عَنِ ابْنِ سِيرِينَ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "ادعوا الله وَأَنْتُمْ مُوقِنُونَ بِالْإِجَابَةِ، وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَسْتَجِيبُ دُعَاءً مِنْ قَلْبٍ غَافِلٍ لَاهٍ" .

---

## 40:15-17 — verses 15-17 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing of His greatness and majesty, and of the elevation of His Mighty Throne, which is exalted above all His creation like a canopy over it, as the Almighty said: {From Allah, the Lord of the ascending stairways. The angels and the Spirit ascend to Him in a Day whose measure is fifty thousand years, so be patient} [al-Ma'arij: 3, 4]. It will be explained later that this is the distance between the Throne and the seventh earth, according to the statement of a group of the salaf (early generations) and the khalaf (later generations), and this is the most likely view, if Allah wills. More than one scholar has mentioned that the Throne is made of red ruby, and that the span between its two ends is a journey of fifty thousand years, and its height above the seventh earth is a journey of fifty thousand years. What has already preceded in the hadith of "al-Aw'al" (the mountain goats) indicates that its elevation above the seven heavens is something immense.

His saying: {He casts the Spirit, by His command, upon whomever He wills of His servants} is like His saying: {He sends down the angels with the Spirit, by His command, upon whomever He wills of His servants, saying: Warn that there is no god except Me, so fear Me} [al-Nahl: 2], and like His saying: {And indeed it is a revelation from the Lord of the worlds. The trustworthy Spirit brought it down. Upon your heart, that you may be of the warners. In a clear Arabic tongue} [al-Shu'ara: 192-194]. And for this reason He said: {That he may warn of the Day of Meeting}. Ali ibn Abi Talha reported from Ibn Abbas: {The Day of Meeting} is one of the names of the Day of Resurrection, by which He warned His servants.

Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abbas said: on that day Adam and the last of his descendants will meet.

Ibn Zayd said: on that day the servants will meet.

Qatadah, al-Suddi, Bilal ibn Sa'd, and Sufyan ibn Uyaynah said: on that day the people of heaven and the people of earth will meet.

Qatadah also said: on that day the people of heaven and the people of earth will meet, and the Creator and the creation.

Maymun ibn Mihran said: on that day the wrongdoer and the wronged will meet.

It may be said that the Day of Resurrection encompasses all of this, and also encompasses the fact that every doer of deeds will meet what he did of good and evil, as others have said.

His saying: {The Day when they are exposed} means: all of them will be visible and exposed, with nothing to shelter them, shade them, or conceal them. For this reason He said: {The Day when they are exposed, nothing of them will be hidden from Allah}, meaning: all of them are equal in His knowledge.

His saying: {To whom belongs the dominion this Day? To Allah, the One, the All-Overpowering} has already been discussed in the hadith of Ibn Umar: that the Almighty will fold up the heavens and the earth with His Hand, then say: I am the King, I am the Compeller, I am the Proud One. Where are the kings of the earth? Where are the compellers? Where are the proud ones?

And in the hadith of the Trumpet: that when the Almighty seizes the souls of all His creation, so that none remains except Him alone, with no partner, He then says: To whom belongs the dominion this Day? three times, then He answers Himself, saying: {To Allah, the One, the All-Overpowering}, meaning: He who alone has overpowered and overcome everything.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ubayd ibn Ubaydah, narrated to us Mu'tamir, from his father, narrated to us Abu Nadrah, from Ibn Abbas (may Allah be pleased with them both), who said: A caller will call out before the Hour: O people, the Hour has come to you. The living and the dead will hear it. He said: And Allah, Mighty and Majestic, will descend to the lowest heaven and say: {To whom belongs the dominion this Day? To Allah, the One, the All-Overpowering}.

His saying: {This Day every soul will be recompensed for what it earned. There is no injustice this Day. Indeed, Allah is swift in reckoning} informs of His justice in His judgment among His creation, that He does not wrong anyone by even the weight of an atom, whether of good or evil. Rather, He rewards a good deed tenfold and a bad deed with its equivalent. For this reason He said: {There is no injustice this Day}, as is established in Sahih Muslim, from Abu Dharr, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, relating from his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, that He said: "O My servants, I have forbidden injustice for Myself and have made it forbidden among you, so do not wrong one another..." until he said: "O My servants, it is only your deeds that I record for you, then I repay you for them in full. So whoever finds good, let him praise Allah, and whoever finds other than that, let him blame no one but himself."

His saying: {Indeed, Allah is swift in reckoning} means: He reckons with all creatures just as He reckons with a single soul, as He said: {Your creation and your resurrection are but as that of a single soul} [Luqman: 28], and He, the Almighty, said: {And Our command is but a single word, like the twinkling of an eye} [al-Qamar: 50].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى [مُخْبِرًا] عَنْ عَظَمَتِهِ وَكِبْرِيَائِهِ، وَارْتِفَاعِ عَرْشِهِ الْعَظِيمِ الْعَالِي عَلَى جَمِيعِ مَخْلُوقَاتِهِ كَالسَّقْفِ لَهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مِنَ اللَّهِ ذِي الْمَعَارِجِ تَعْرُجُ الْمَلائِكَةُ وَالرُّوحُ إِلَيْهِ فِي يَوْمٍ كَانَ مِقْدَارُهُ خَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ [فَاصْبِرْ] ﴾ [الْمَعَارِجِ:٣، ٤] ، وَسَيَأْتِي بَيَانُ أَنَّ هَذِهِ مَسَافَةُ مَا بَيْنَ الْعَرْشِ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ السَّابِعَةِ، فِي قَوْلِ جَمَاعَةٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ، وَهُوَ الْأَرْجَحُ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] . وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ أَنَّ الْعَرْشَ مِنْ يَاقُوتَةٍ حَمْرَاءَ، اتِّسَاعُ مَا بَيْنَ قُطْرَيْهِ مَسِيرَةَ خَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ. وَارْتِفَاعُهُ عَنِ الْأَرْضِ السَّابِعَةِ مَسِيرَةَ خَمْسِينَ أَلْفَ سَنَةٍ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي حَدِيثِ "الْأَوْعَالِ" مَا يَدُلُّ عَلَى ارْتِفَاعِهِ عن السموات السَّبْعِ بِشَيْءٍ عَظِيمٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يُلْقِي الرُّوحَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِ عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يُنزلُ الْمَلائِكَةَ بِالرُّوحِ مِنْ أَمْرِهِ عَلَى مَنْ يَشَاءُ مِنْ عِبَادِهِ أَنْ أَنْذِرُوا أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا أَنَا [فَاتَّقُونِ] ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ٢] ، وَكَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِنَّهُ لَتَنزيلُ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ. نزلَ بِهِ الرُّوحُ الأمِينُ. عَلَى قَلْبِكَ لِتَكُونَ مِنَ الْمُنْذِرِينَ. [بِلِسَانٍ عَرَبِيٍّ مُبِين] ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ١٩٢ -١٩٤] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لِيُنْذِرَ يَوْمَ التَّلاقِ﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿يَوْمَ التَّلاقِ﴾ اسْمٌ مِنْ أَسْمَاءِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، حَذَّرَ مِنْهُ عِبَادَهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيج: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَلْتَقِي فِيهِ آدَمُ وَآخِرُ وَلَدِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: يَلْتَقِي فِيهِ الْعِبَادُ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَبِلَالُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، وَسُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ : يَلْتَقِي فِيهِ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ وَأَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ أَيْضًا: يَلْتَقِي فِيهِ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ وَأَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ، وَالْخَالِقُ وَالْخَلْقُ.

وَقَالَ مَيْمون بْنُ مِهْران: يَلْتَقِي [فِيهِ] الظَّالِمُ وَالْمَظْلُومُ.

وَقَدْ يُقَالُ: إِنَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ هُوَ يَشْمَلُ هَذَا كُلَّهُ، وَيَشْمَلُ أَنَّ كُلَّ عَامِلٍ سَيَلْقَى مَا عَمِلَ مِنْ خَيْرٍ وَشَرٍّ. كَمَا قَالَهُ آخَرُونَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَوْمَ هُمْ بَارِزُونَ﴾ أَيْ: ظَاهِرُونَ بَادُونَ كُلُّهُمْ، لَا شَيْءَ يُكِنُّهُمْ وَلَا يُظِلُّهُمْ وَلَا يَسْتُرُهُمْ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَوْمَ هُمْ بَارِزُونَ لَا يَخْفَى عَلَى اللَّهِ مِنْهُمْ شَيْءٌ﴾ أَيِ: الْجَمِيعُ فِي عِلْمِهِ عَلَى السَّوَاءِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِمَنِ الْمُلْكُ الْيَوْمَ لِلَّهِ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي حَدِيثِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ: أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى يَطْوِي السموات وَالْأَرْضَ بِيَدِهِ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: أَنَا الْمَلِكُ، أَنَا الْجَبَّارُ، أَنَا الْمُتَكَبِّرُ، أَيْنَ مُلُوكُ الْأَرْضِ؟ أَيْنَ الْجَبَّارُونَ؟ أَيْنَ الْمُتَكَبِّرُونَ؟ .

وَفِي حَدِيثِ الصُّورِ: أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى إِذَا قَبَضَ أَرْوَاحَ جَمِيعِ خَلْقِهِ، فَلَمْ يَبْقَ سِوَاهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، حِينَئِذٍ يَقُولُ: لِمَنِ الْمَلِكُ الْيَوْمَ؟ ثَلَاثَ مَرَّاتٍ، ثُمَّ يُجِيبُ نَفْسَهُ قَائِلًا ﴿لِلَّهِ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي هُوَ وَحْدَهُ قَدْ قَهَر كُلَّ شَيْءٍ وَغَلَبَهُ .

وَقَدْ قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ غَالِبٍ الدَّقَّاقُ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ بْنُ عُبَيْدَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُعْتَمِرٌ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو نَضْرة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] قَالَ: يُنَادِي مُنَادٍ بَيْنَ يَدَيِ السَّاعَةِ: يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، أَتَتْكُمُ السَّاعَةُ. فَيَسْمَعُهَا الْأَحْيَاءُ وَالْأَمْوَاتُ، قَالَ: وَيَنْزِلُ اللَّهُ [عَزَّ وَجَلَّ] إِلَى سَمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا وَيَقُولُ: ﴿لِمَنِ الْمُلْكُ الْيَوْمَ لِلَّهِ الْوَاحِدِ الْقَهَّارِ﴾ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿الْيَوْمَ تُجْزَى كُلُّ نَفْسٍ بِمَا كَسَبَتْ لَا ظُلْمَ الْيَوْمَ إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عَدْلِهِ فِي حُكْمِهِ بَيْنَ خَلْقِهِ، أَنَّهُ لَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ مِنْ خَيْرٍ وَلَا مِنْ شَرٍّ، بَلْ يَجْزِي بِالْحَسَنَةِ عَشْرَ أَمْثَالِهَا، وَبِالسَّيِّئَةِ وَاحِدَةً؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا ظُلْمَ الْيَوْمَ﴾ كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ ، عَنْ أَبِي ذَرٍّ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ -فِيمَا يَحْكِي عَنْ رَبِّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "يَا عِبَادِي، إِنِّي حَرَّمْتُ الظُّلْمَ عَلَى نَفْسِي وَجَعَلْتُهُ بَيْنَكُمْ مُحَرَّمًا فَلَا تَظَالَمُوا -إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ-: يَا عِبَادِي، إِنَّمَا هِيَ أَعْمَالُكُمْ أُحْصِيهَا عَلَيْكُمْ ثُمَّ أُوَفِّيكُمْ إِيَّاهَا، فَمَنْ وَجَدَ خَيْرًا فَلْيَحْمَدِ اللَّهَ، ومن وجد غير ذلك فلا يلومن إلا نَفْسَهُ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ﴾ أَيْ: يُحَاسِبُ الْخَلَائِقَ كُلَّهُمْ، كَمَا يُحَاسِبُ نَفْسًا وَاحِدَةً، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿مَا خَلْقُكُمْ وَلا بَعْثُكُمْ إِلا كَنَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٢٨] ، وَقَالَ [تَعَالَى] : ﴿وَمَا أَمْرُنَا إِلا وَاحِدَةٌ كَلَمْحٍ بِالْبَصَرِ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ٥٠] .

---

## 40:18-20 — verses 18-20 (shared commentary)

### Translation

"The Day of the Impending" is a name from among the names of the Day of Resurrection. It was named thus because of its nearness, as He, exalted, said: {The impending has drawn near. It has, besides God, no remover} [al-Najm: 57-58]. And He said: {The Hour has drawn near and the moon has split} [al-Qamar: 1]. And He said: {The reckoning of the people has drawn near for them} [al-Anbiya: 1]. And He said: {The command of God has come, so do not seek to hasten it} [al-Nahl: 1]. And He said: {But when they see it drawing near, the faces of those who disbelieved will turn wretched, and it will be said: This is that which you used to claim} [al-Mulk: 27].

Regarding His saying: {When the hearts are at the throats, kazimin (choked, silent)}, that is, silent. Qatadah said: the hearts come to a halt in the throats out of fear, so they neither come out nor return to their places. Ikrimah, al-Suddi, and others said the same.

The meaning of {kazimin} is: silent, no one speaks except by His permission: {The Day the Spirit and the angels will stand in ranks, they will not speak except one whom the Merciful permits, and he will say what is correct} [al-Naba: 38].

Ibn Jurayj said: {kazimin} means: weeping.

Regarding His saying: {The wrongdoers will have no intimate friend and no intercessor who is obeyed}, that is, those who wronged themselves through associating partners with God have no near one among them who can benefit them, and no intercessor who is granted intercession on their behalf. Rather, all means of connection to any good have been severed for them.

Regarding His saying: {He knows the treachery of the eyes and what the breasts conceal}, He, exalted, informs of His complete knowledge encompassing all things, the great and the small, the little and the large, the fine and the subtle, so that people should be wary of His knowledge concerning them, and thereby feel true shame before God, and fear Him with true fear, and watch themselves as one who knows he is being watched. For He, exalted, knows the treacherous eye even if it displays trustworthiness, and He knows what the hidden matters of the breasts conceal of inner thoughts and secrets.

Ibn Abbas said regarding His saying: {He knows the treachery of the eyes and what the breasts conceal}, it refers to a man who enters upon a household, and among them is a beautiful woman, or a beautiful woman passes by him and them. When they are inattentive, he glances at her, and when they notice, he lowers [his gaze from her]. When they are inattentive again, he glances, and when they notice, he lowers [his gaze from her], while God has already seen from his heart that he wished he could gaze upon her private parts. Narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim.

Al-Dahhak said: {the treachery of the eyes} is the covert signal, and a man's saying "I saw" when he did not see, or "I did not see" when he did see.

Ibn Abbas said: God, exalted, knows from the eye in its glance whether it intends treachery or not. Mujahid and Qatadah said the same.

Ibn Abbas said regarding His saying: {and what the breasts conceal}, He knows, if you were able to reach her, whether you would commit adultery with her or not.

Al-Suddi said: {and what the breasts conceal} means: of whispering temptation.

Regarding His saying: {And God judges with truth}, that is, He rules with justice.

Al-A'mash reported from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with them both, regarding His saying: {And God judges with truth}: He is able to reward good with good and evil with evil. {Indeed God is the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing}.

This interpretation which Ibn Abbas gave for this verse is like His saying, exalted: {That He may recompense those who do evil for what they have done, and recompense those who do good with what is best} [al-Najm: 31]. And His saying: {And those they call upon besides Him}, that is, of idols, false gods, and rivals, {do not judge anything}, that is, they possess nothing and rule over nothing. {Indeed God is the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing}, that is, He hears the words of His creation and sees them, so He guides whom He wills and leads astray whom He wills, and He is the just judge in all of that.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَوْمَ الْآزِفَةِ هُوَ: اسْمٌ مِنْ أَسْمَاءِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ، سُمِّيَتْ بِذَلِكَ لِاقْتِرَابِهَا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَزِفَتِ الآزِفَةُ. لَيْسَ لَهَا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ كَاشِفَةٌ﴾ [النَّجْمِ:٥٧، ٥٨] وَقَالَ ﴿اقْتَرَبَتِ السَّاعَةُ وَانْشَقَّ الْقَمَرُ﴾ [الْقَمَرِ: ١] ، وَقَالَ ﴿اقْتَرَبَ لِلنَّاسِ حِسَابُهُمْ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ:١] وَقَالَ ﴿أَتَى أَمْرُ اللَّهِ فَلا تَسْتَعْجِلُوهُ﴾ [النَّحْلِ:١] وَقَالَ ﴿فَلَمَّا رَأَوْهُ زُلْفَةً سِيئَتْ وُجُوهُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَقِيلَ هَذَا الَّذِي كُنْتُمْ بِهِ تَدَّعُونَ﴾ [الْمُلْكِ:٢٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِذِ الْقُلُوبُ لَدَى الْحَنَاجِرِ كَاظِمِينَ﴾ [أَيْ سَاكِتِينَ] ، قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَقَفَتِ الْقُلُوبُ فِي الْحَنَاجِرِ مِنَ الْخَوْفِ، فَلَا تَخْرُجُ وَلَا تَعُودُ إِلَى أَمَاكِنِهَا. وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَمَعْنَى ﴿كَاظِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: سَاكِتِينَ، لَا يَتَكَلَّمُ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِهِ ﴿يَوْمَ يَقُومُ الرُّوحُ وَالْمَلائِكَةُ صَفًّا لَا يَتَكَلَّمُونَ إِلا مَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ الرَّحْمَنُ وَقَالَ صَوَابًا﴾ [النَّبَأِ:٣٨] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج : ﴿كَاظِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: بَاكِينَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا لِلظَّالِمِينَ مِنْ حَمِيمٍ وَلا شَفِيعٍ يُطَاعُ﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ لِلَّذِينِ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ بِالشِّرْكِ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ قَرِيبٍ مِنْهُمْ يَنْفَعُهُمْ، وَلَا شَفِيعٍ يُشَفَّعُ فِيهِمْ، بَلْ قَدْ تَقَطَّعَتْ بِهِمُ الْأَسْبَابُ مِنْ كُلِّ خَيْرٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَعْلَمُ خَائِنَةَ الأعْيُنِ وَمَا تُخْفِي الصُّدُورُ﴾ يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ عِلْمِهِ التَّامِّ الْمُحِيطِ بِجَمِيعِ الْأَشْيَاءِ، جَلِيلِهَا وَحَقِيرِهَا، صَغِيرِهَا وَكَبِيرِهَا، دَقِيقِهَا وَلَطِيفِهَا؛ لِيَحْذَرَ النَّاسُ عِلْمَهُ فِيهِمْ، فَيَسْتَحْيُوا مِنَ اللَّهِ حَقّ الْحَيَاءِ، ويَتَّقُوهُ حَقَّ تَقْوَاهُ، وَيُرَاقِبُوهُ مُرَاقَبَةَ مَنْ يَعْلَمُ أَنَّهُ يَرَاهُ، فَإِنَّهُ تَعَالَى يَعْلَمُ الْعَيْنَ الْخَائِنَةَ وَإِنْ أَبْدَتْ أَمَانَةً، وَيَعْلَمُ مَا تَنْطَوِي عَلَيْهِ خَبَايَا الصُّدُورِ مِنَ الضَّمَائِرِ وَالسَّرَائِرِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿يَعْلَمُ خَائِنَةَ الأعْيُنِ وَمَا تُخْفِي الصُّدُورُ﴾ وَهُوَ الرَّجُلُ يَدْخُلُ عَلَى أَهْلِ الْبَيْتِ بَيْتَهُمْ، وَفِيهِمُ الْمَرْأَةُ الْحَسْنَاءُ، أَوْ تَمُرُّ بِهِ وَبِهِمُ الْمَرْأَةُ الْحَسْنَاءُ، فَإِذَا غَفَلُوا لَحَظَ إِلَيْهَا، فَإِذَا فَطِنُوا غَضّ، فَإِذَا غَفَلُوا لَحَظَ، فَإِذَا فَطِنُوا غَضَّ [بَصَرَهُ عَنْهَا] وَقَدِ اطَّلَعَ اللَّهُ مِنْ قَلْبِهِ أَنَّهُ وَدّ أَنْ لَوِ اطَّلَعَ عَلَى فَرْجِهَا. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿خَائِنَةَ الأعْيُنِ﴾ هُوَ الْغَمْزُ، وَقَوْلُ الرَّجُلِ: رَأَيْتُ، وَلَمْ يَرَ؛ أَوْ: لَمْ أَرَ، وَقَدْ رَأَى.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْلَمُ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى مِنَ الْعَيْنِ فِي نَظَرِهَا، هَلْ تُرِيدُ الْخِيَانَةَ أَمْ لَا؟ وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا تُخْفِي الصُّدُورُ﴾ يَعْلَمُ إِذَا أَنْتَ قَدَرْتَ عَلَيْهَا هَلْ تَزْنِي بِهَا أَمْ لَا؟.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿وَمَا تُخْفِي الصُّدُورُ﴾ أي: من الوسوسة.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ يَقْضِي بِالْحَقِّ﴾ أَيْ: يَحْكُمُ بِالْعَدْلِ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشِ: عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ يَقْضِي بِالْحَقِّ﴾ قَادِرٌ عَلَى أَنْ يَجْزِيَ بِالْحَسَنَةِ الْحَسَنَةَ، وَبِالسَّيِّئَةِ السَّيِّئَةَ ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْبَصِيرُ﴾ .

وَهَذَا الَّذِي فَسَّرَ بِهِ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿لِيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَسَاءُوا بِمَا عَمِلُوا وَيَجْزِيَ الَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا بِالْحُسْنَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٣١] . وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ مِنْ دُونِهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَوْثَانِ وَالْأَنْدَادِ، ﴿لَا يَقْضُونَ بِشَيْءٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَمْلِكُونَ شَيْئًا وَلَا يَحْكُمُونَ بِشَيْءٍ ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْبَصِيرُ﴾ أَيْ: سَمِيعٌ لِأَقْوَالِ خَلْقِهِ، بَصِيرٌ بِهِمْ، فَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَشَاءُ، وَيُضِلُّ مَنْ يَشَاءُ، وَهُوَ الْحَاكِمُ الْعَادِلُ فِي جَمِيعِ ذَلِكَ.

---

## 40:21-22 — verses 21-22 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, the Exalted, says: Have these deniers of your message, O Muhammad, not traveled {through the land and observed how the end was for those who came before them}, that is, of the nations who denied the prophets, what befell them of punishment and exemplary chastisement, even though they were greater than these people in strength {and in the traces they left in the land}, that is, they left behind constructions, landmarks, and dwellings in the earth that these people are incapable of achieving, as He said: {And We had certainly established them in such as We have not established you} [al-Ahqaf: 26], and He said: {and they cultivated the land and built it up more than these have built it up} [al-Rum: 9]. That is, despite this tremendous strength and severe might, God seized them for their sins, which was their disbelief in their messengers, {and they had no protector against God}, meaning no one warded off God's punishment from them, no one repelled it from them, and no protector shielded them.

Then He mentions the reason for His seizing them and the sins which they committed and perpetrated, saying: {That was because their messengers used to come to them with clear proofs}, that is, with manifest evidences and decisive proofs, {but they disbelieved}, meaning that despite this clarity and proof they disbelieved and rejected, {so God seized them}, that is, He destroyed them and brought ruin upon them, and for the disbelievers there are similar fates, {indeed He is Strong, severe in punishment}, meaning He possesses tremendous strength and severe might, and He is {severe in punishment}, meaning His punishment is painful, severe, and agonizing. May God protect us from it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يقول تعالى: أو لم يَسِرْ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُكَذِّبُونَ بِرِسَالَتِكَ يَا مُحَمَّدُ ﴿فِي الأرْضِ فَيَنْظُرُوا كَيْفَ كَانَ عَاقِبَةُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ بِالْأَنْبِيَاءِ، مَا حَلَّ بِهِمْ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا أَشَدَّ مِنْ هَؤُلَاءِ قُوَّةً ﴿وَآثَارًا فِي الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: أَثَّرُوا فِي الْأَرْضِ مِنَ الْبِنَايَاتِ وَالْمَعَالِمِ وَالدِّيَارَاتِ، مَا لَا يَقْدِرُ عَلَيْهِ هَؤُلَاءِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ مَكَّنَّاهُمْ فِيمَا إِنْ مَكَّنَّاكُمْ فِيهِ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ: ٢٦] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَأَثَارُوا الأرْضَ وَعَمَرُوهَا أَكْثَرَ مِمَّا عَمَرُوهَا﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٩] أَيْ: وَمَعَ هَذِهِ الْقُوَّةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ وَالْبَأْسِ الشَّدِيدِ، أَخَذَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ، وَهِيَ كُفْرُهُمْ بِرُسُلِهِمْ، ﴿وَمَا كَانَ لَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنْ وَاقٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا دَفَعَ عَنْهُمْ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ أَحَدٌ، وَلَا رَدَّهُ عَنْهُمْ رَادٌّ، وَلَا وَقَاهُمْ وَاقٍ.

ثُمَّ ذَكَرَ عِلَّةَ أَخْذِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ وَذُنُوبَهُمُ الَّتِي ارْتَكَبُوهَا وَاجْتَرَمُوهَا، فَقَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ كَانَتْ تَأْتِيهِمْ رُسُلُهُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالدَّلَائِلِ الْوَاضِحَاتِ وَالْبَرَاهِينِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ، ﴿فَكَفَرُوا﴾ أَيْ: مَعَ هَذَا الْبَيَانِ وَالْبُرْهَانِ كَفَرُوا وَجَحَدُوا، ﴿فَأَخَذَهُمُ اللَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: أَهْلَكَهُمْ ودمَّر عَلَيْهِمْ وَلِلْكَافِرِينَ أَمْثَالُهَا، ﴿إِنَّهُ قَوِيٌّ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ﴾ أَيْ: ذُو قُوَّةٍ عَظِيمَةٍ وَبَطْشٍ شَدِيدٍ، وَهُوَ ﴿شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ﴾ أَيْ: عِقَابُهُ أَلِيمٌ شَدِيدٌ وَجِيعٌ. أَعَاذَنَا اللَّهُ مِنْهُ.

---

## 40:23-27 — verses 23-27 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, consoling His Prophet ﷺ regarding the denial of those among his people who denied him, and giving him glad tidings that the final outcome and victory would be his in this world and the next, just as happened with Musa ibn Imran (peace be upon him). For God Almighty sent him with clear signs and manifest proofs. Hence He said: {With Our signs and manifest authority}, and al-sultan (authority) here means proof and evidence.

{To Fir'awn} who was the king of the Copts in the land of Egypt, {and Haman} who was his minister in his kingdom, {and Qarun} who was the wealthiest of people in his time in property and trade. {And they said, a magician, a great liar}, meaning: they denied him and made him out to be a deceptive, deluding sorcerer, a great liar regarding the claim that God had sent him. This is like His saying: {Thus there came no messenger to those before them except that they said, a magician or a madman. Did they enjoin this upon one another? Rather, they are a transgressing people} [al-Dhariyat 52-53].

{But when he brought them the truth from Us}, meaning: with the decisive proof indicating that God Almighty had sent him to them, {they said, kill the sons of those who believed with him and let their women live}. This is a second order from Fir'awn to kill the male children of the Children of Israel. As for the first order, it was to guard against the emergence of Musa, or to humiliate this people and reduce their numbers, or for both reasons combined. As for the second order, it was for the second reason: to humiliate this people and so that they would take Musa (peace be upon him) as an omen of ill fortune. Hence they said: {We were harmed before you came to us and after you came to us. He said, perhaps your Lord will destroy your enemy and make you successors in the land, then He will observe how you act} [al-A'raf: 129].

Qatadah said: This is one command after another.

God Almighty said: {And the plot of the disbelievers is not but in error}, meaning: their scheming and their aim, which was to reduce the numbers of the Children of Israel so that they would not be granted victory over them, would come to nothing and perish in error.

{And Fir'awn said, leave me to kill Musa, and let him call upon his Lord}. This is a resolve on the part of Fir'awn, may God curse him, to kill Musa (peace be upon him), meaning: he said to his people, leave me be so that I may kill this man for you. {And let him call upon his Lord}, meaning: I do not fear him at all. This represents the utmost degree of denial, insolent defiance, and obstinacy.

His statement, may God disfigure him: {Indeed, I fear that he will change your religion or that he will cause corruption to appear in the land}, referring to Musa. Fir'awn feared that Musa would lead the people astray and change their customs and traditions. This is like the proverb that says, "Fir'awn has become a preacher," meaning an admonisher, showing concern for the people regarding Musa (peace be upon him).

Most reciters read it as: "that he will change your religion and that he will cause corruption to appear in the land," while others read: {or that he will cause corruption to appear in the land}, and some of them read "corruption" (al-fasadu) with a nominative ending, making it the subject of "appear."

Musa said: {Indeed, I have sought refuge in my Lord and your Lord from every arrogant one who does not believe in the Day of Reckoning}, meaning: when the statement of Fir'awn, {leave me to kill Musa}, reached him, Musa said: I have sought protection with God and taken refuge in Him from his evil and the evil of his like. Hence he said: {Indeed, I have sought refuge in my Lord and your Lord}, O you who are being addressed, {from every arrogant one}, meaning: one who turns away from the truth, a criminal, {who does not believe in the Day of Reckoning}. Hence there comes in the hadith from Abu Musa, may God be pleased with him, that the Messenger of God ﷺ, when he feared a people, would say: "O God, we seek refuge in You from their evils, and we place You before their throats [as a shield against them]."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُسَلِّيًا لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ فِي تَكْذِيبِ مَنْ كَذَّبَهُ مِنْ قَوْمِهُ، وَمُبَشِّرًا لَهُ بِأَنَّ الْعَاقِبَةَ وَالنُّصْرَةَ لَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، كَمَا جَرَى لِمُوسَى بْنِ عِمْرَانَ ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَرْسَلَهُ بِالْآيَاتِ الْبَيِّنَاتِ، وَالدَّلَائِلِ الْوَاضِحَاتِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿بِآيَاتِنَا وَسُلْطَانٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ وَالسُّلْطَانُ هُوَ: الحُجة وَالْبُرْهَانُ.

﴿إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ﴾ هُوَ: مَلِكُ الْقِبْطِ بِالدِّيَارِ الْمِصْرِيَّةِ، ﴿وَهَامَانَ﴾ وَهُوَ: وَزِيرُهُ فِي مَمْلَكَتِهِ ﴿وَقَارُونَ﴾ وَكَانَ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ فِي زَمَانِهِ مَالًا وَتِجَارَةً ﴿فَقَالُوا سَاحِرٌ كَذَّابٌ﴾ أَيْ: كَذَّبُوهُ وَجَعَلُوهُ سَاحِرًا مُمَخْرِقًا مُمَوِّهًا كَذَّابًا فِي أَنَّ اللَّهَ أَرْسَلَهُ. وَهَذِهِ كَقَوْلِهِ [تَعَالَى] : ﴿كَذَلِكَ مَا أَتَى الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا قَالُوا سَاحِرٌ أَوْ مَجْنُونٌ أَتَوَاصَوْا بِهِ بَلْ هُمْ قَوْمٌ طَاغُونَ﴾ [الذَّارِيَاتِ ٥٢، ٥٣] .

﴿فَلَمَّا جَاءَهُمْ بِالْحَقِّ مِنْ عِنْدِنَا﴾ أَيْ: بِالْبُرْهَانِ الْقَاطِعِ الدَّالِّ عَلَى أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَرْسَلَهُ إِلَيْهِمْ، ﴿قَالُوا اقْتُلُوا أَبْنَاءَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ وَاسْتَحْيُوا نِسَاءَهُمْ﴾ وَهَذَا أَمْرٌ ثَانٍ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ بِقَتْلِ ذُكُورِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ. أَمَّا الْأَوَّلُ: فَكَانَ لِأَجْلِ الِاحْتِرَازِ مِنْ وُجُودِ مُوسَى، أَوْ لِإِذْلَالِ هَذَا الشَّعْبِ وَتَقْلِيلِ عَدَدِهِمْ، أَوْ لِمَجْمُوعِ الْأَمْرَيْنِ. وَأَمَّا الْأَمْرُ الثَّانِي: فَلِلْعِلَّةِ الثَّانِيَةِ، لِإِهَانَةِ هَذَا الشَّعْبِ، وَلِكَيْ يَتَشَاءَمُوا بِمُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿أُوذِينَا مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تَأْتِيَنَا وَمِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جِئْتَنَا قَالَ عَسَى رَبُّكُمْ أَنْ يُهْلِكَ عَدُوَّكُمْ وَيَسْتَخْلِفَكُمْ فِي الأرْضِ فَيَنْظُرَ كَيْفَ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٢٩] .

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هَذَا أَمْرٌ بَعْدَ أَمْرٍ.

قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كَيْدُ الْكَافِرِينَ إِلا فِي ضَلالٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا مَكْرُهُمْ وَقَصْدُهُمُ الَّذِي هُوَ تَقْلِيلُ عَدَدِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ لِئَلَّا يُنصروا عَلَيْهِمْ، إِلَّا ذَاهِبٌ وَهَالِكٌ فِي ضَلَالٍ.
