﴿وَقَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ ذَرُونِي أَقْتُلْ مُوسَى وَلْيَدْعُ رَبَّهُ﴾ وَهَذَا عَزْمٌ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ -لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ-عَلَى قَتْلِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَيْ: قَالَ لِقَوْمِهِ: دَعُونِي حَتَّى أَقْتُلَ لَكُمْ هَذَا، ﴿وَلْيَدْعُ رَبَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: لَا أُبَالِي مِنْهُ. وَهَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْجَحْدِ وَالتَّجَهْرُمِ وَالْعِنَادِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ -قَبَّحَهُ اللَّهُ-: ﴿إِنِّي أَخَافُ أَنْ يُبَدِّلَ دِينَكُمْ أَوْ أَنْ يُظْهِرَ فِي الأرْضِ الْفَسَادَ﴾ يَعْنِي: مُوسَى، يَخْشَى فِرْعَوْنُ أَنْ يُضِلَّ مُوسَى النَّاسَ وَيُغَيِّرَ رُسُومَهُمْ وَعَادَاتِهُمْ. وَهَذَا كَمَا يُقَالُ فِي الْمَثَلِ: "صَارَ فِرْعَوْنُ مُذَكِّرًا" يَعْنِي: وَاعِظًا، يُشْفِقُ عَلَى النَّاسِ مِنْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

وَقَرَأَ الْأَكْثَرُونَ: "أَنْ يُبَدِّلَ دِينَكُمْ وَأَنْ يُظهِر فِي الْأَرْضِ الْفَسَادَ" وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: ﴿أَوْ أَنْ يُظْهِرَ فِي الأرْضِ الْفَسَادَ﴾ وَقَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ: "يَظْهَر فِي الْأَرْضِ الفسادُ" بِالضَّمِّ.

وَقَالَ مُوسَى: ﴿إِنِّي عُذْتُ بِرَبِّي وَرَبِّكُمْ مِنْ كُلِّ مُتَكَبِّرٍ لَا يُؤْمِنُ بِيَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ﴾ أَيْ: لَمَّا بَلَغَهُ قَوْلُ فِرْعَوْنَ: ﴿ذَرُونِي أَقْتُلْ مُوسَى﴾ قَالَ مُوسَى: استجرتُ بِاللَّهِ وعُذْتُ بِهِ مِنْ شَرِّهِ وَشَرِّ أَمْثَالِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿إِنِّي عُذْتُ بِرَبِّي وَرَبِّكُمْ﴾ أَيُّهَا الْمُخَاطَبُونَ، ﴿مِنْ كُلِّ مُتَكَبِّرٍ﴾ أَيْ: عَنِ الْحَقِّ، مجرم، ﴿لا يُؤْمِنُ بِيَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ﴾ ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ إِذَا خَافَ قَوْمًا قَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ، إِنَّا نَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ شُرُورِهِمْ، وَنَدْرَأُ بِكَ فِي نُحُورِهِمْ" .

---

## 40:28-29 — verses 28-29 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The well known view is that this believing man was a Copt from the family of Pharaoh.

Al-Suddi said: He was the cousin of Pharaoh, and it is said that he was the one who was saved along with Musa. Ibn Jarir preferred this, and rejected the view of those who held that he was an Israelite, because Pharaoh was affected by his speech and listened to it, and refrained from killing Musa (peace be upon him), whereas had he been an Israelite, Pharaoh would have been quick to punish him, since he was one of them.

Ibn Jurayj reported from Ibn Abbas: none from the family of Pharaoh believed except this man and Pharaoh's wife, and it was he who said: {O Musa, indeed the assembly are conspiring to kill you} [al-Qasas: 20]. This was narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim.

This man used to conceal his faith from his people, the Copts, and it did not become manifest except on this day, when Pharaoh said: {Leave me to kill Musa}. At that a fit of anger for the sake of God, mighty and exalted, seized the man. "The best jihad is a word of justice before a tyrannical ruler," as is established in the hadith, and there was no word greater than this before Pharaoh, which is his saying: {Would you kill a man for saying, my Lord is God} [that is, for the reason that he says, my Lord is God], unless it be what al-Bukhari narrated in his Sahih, where he said:

[chain] Urwah ibn al-Zubayr said: I said to Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As, tell me of the harshest thing that the polytheists did to the Messenger of God ﷺ. He said: While the Messenger of God ﷺ was praying in the courtyard of the Ka'bah, Uqbah ibn Abi Mu'ayt came forward, seized the shoulder of the Messenger of God ﷺ, and twisted his garment around his neck, choking him severely. Then Abu Bakr, may God be pleased with him, came forward, took hold of his shoulder, and pushed him away from the Prophet ﷺ, then said: {Would you kill a man for saying, my Lord is God, when he has brought you clear proofs from your Lord}.

Al-Bukhari narrated this alone from the hadith of al-Awza'i. He said: Muhammad ibn Ishaq followed him in this, from Yahya ibn Urwah, from his father, with the same content.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Amr ibn al-As was asked: what is the harshest thing you saw Quraysh do to the Messenger of God ﷺ? He said: One day he passed by them and they said to him, do you forbid us from worshipping what our forefathers worshipped? He said, "I am the one who does that." So they rose up against him and seized the folds of his garment. I saw Abu Bakr embracing him from behind, crying out at the top of his voice, with his eyes flowing with tears, saying: O my people, {Would you kill a man for saying, my Lord is God, when he has brought you clear proofs from your Lord}, until he finished the entire verse.

Al-Nasa'i likewise narrated this from the hadith of Abdah, making it part of the musnad of Amr ibn al-As, may God be pleased with him.

His saying: {when he has brought you clear proofs from your Lord}, that is: how can you kill a man for saying, "my Lord is God," when he has established for you the proof of the truth of what he brought you? Then he descended to their level in addressing them and said: {And if he is lying, then upon him is his lie, but if he is truthful, some of what he promises you will befall you}, meaning: even if he has not shown you clearly the soundness of what he brought, it is a matter of reason, sound judgment, and prudence that you leave him and his own affair alone, and not harm him. For if he is lying, God will requite him for his lie with punishment in this world and the next, and if he is truthful, and you have harmed him, then some of what he threatens you with will befall you, for he threatens you, should you oppose him, with punishment in this world and the next. Since it is possible, in your view, that he may be truthful, it follows that you ought not to confront him, but rather leave him and his people, letting him call them and them follow him.

Thus God, exalted is He, informed us about Musa (peace be upon him), that he sought from Pharaoh and his people a truce, in His saying: {And We had already tried before them the people of Pharaoh, and there came to them a noble messenger, saying: Deliver to me the servants of God, indeed I am to you a trustworthy messenger, and do not exalt yourselves above God, indeed I bring you clear authority, and indeed I have sought refuge in my Lord and your Lord, lest you stone me, and if you do not believe me, then leave me alone} [al-Dukhan: 17-21]. Likewise the Messenger of God ﷺ said to Quraysh that they should leave him to call the servants of God to God, exalted is He, and not touch him with harm, and that they should honor the bond of kinship between him and them by refraining from harming him. God, exalted is He, said: {Say: I do not ask you for it any reward, except love for kinship} [al-Shura: 23], meaning: except that you not harm me on account of the kinship between me and you, so do not harm me, and leave the matter between me and the people. It was upon this basis that the truce of al-Hudaybiyyah was concluded, and it was a manifest victory.

His saying: {Indeed, God does not guide one who is transgressing and a liar}, that is: if this one who claims that God sent him to you were a liar, as you claim, then his affair would be plainly manifest, evident to everyone in his words and deeds, which would be in the utmost state of contradiction and confusion. Yet we see his affair to be sound and his path to be upright, and had he been among the transgressing liars, God would not have guided him, nor directed him to what you see of the order and coherence of his affair and conduct.

Then the believer said, warning his people against the removal of God's favor from them and the descent of God's punishment upon them: {O my people, sovereignty is yours today, dominant in the land}, that is: God has favored you with this sovereignty and dominance in the land, with commanding authority and broad standing, so guard this favor by giving thanks to God and believing His messenger ﷺ, and beware of God's punishment if you deny His messenger. {Then who will help us against the punishment of God, should it come to us}, that is: these armies and these forces will not avail you anything, nor will they repel from us any part of God's punishment, should He intend evil against us.

{Pharaoh said}, to his people, in rebuttal of what this righteous, dutiful, rightly-guided man, who was more deserving of sovereignty than Pharaoh, had counseled: {I do not show you except what I see}, that is: I say to you and counsel you nothing but what I see fit for myself. And Pharaoh lied, for he in fact recognized the truth of Musa in what he brought of the message: {He said, you have already known that none has sent these down except the Lord of the heavens and the earth as insights} [al-Isra: 102]. And God, exalted is He, said: {And they rejected them, while their souls were convinced of them, out of injustice and arrogance} [al-Naml: 14].

So his saying: {I do not show you except what I see} was a lie and a fabrication on his part, and he betrayed God, His messenger, and his subjects, deceiving them and giving them no sincere counsel. Likewise his saying: {and I do not guide you except to the way of right conduct}, that is: I call you to nothing but the path of truth, honesty, and right guidance, was also a lie on his part, even though his people obeyed him and followed him. God, exalted is He, said: {So they followed the command of Pharaoh, and the command of Pharaoh was not rightly guided} [Hud: 97]. And He, exalted is He, said: {And Pharaoh led his people astray, and did not guide them rightly} [Taha: 79]. And in the hadith: "There is no ruler who dies on the day he dies while he is deceiving his subjects, except that he will not smell the fragrance of Paradise, though its fragrance can be found from a distance of five hundred years' journey."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

الْمَشْهُورُ أَنَّ هَذَا الرَّجُلَ الْمُؤْمِنَ كَانَ قبْطيًا مِنْ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ.

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: كَانَ ابْنَ عَمِّ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَيُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ الَّذِي نَجَا مَعَ مُوسَى. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ ، وَرَدَّ قَوْلَ مَنْ ذَهَبَ إِلَى أَنَّهُ كَانَ إِسْرَائِيلِيًّا؛ لِأَنَّ فِرْعَوْنَ انْفَعَلَ لِكَلَامِهِ وَاسْتَمَعَهُ، وَكَفَّ عَنْ قَتْلِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَلَوْ كَانَ إِسْرَائِيلِيًّا لَأَوْشَكَ أَنْ يُعَاجَلَ بِالْعُقُوبَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ مِنْهُمْ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيج عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: لَمْ يُؤْمَنْ مِنْ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ سِوَى هَذَا الرَّجُلِ وَامْرَأَةِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَالَّذِي قَالَ: ﴿يَا مُوسَى إِنَّ الْمَلأ يَأْتَمِرُونَ بِكَ لِيَقْتُلُوكَ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ:٢٠] رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

وَقَدْ كَانَ هَذَا الرجلُ يَكْتُمُ إِيمَانَهُ عَنْ قَوْمِهِ الْقِبْطِ، فَلَمْ يَظْهَرْ إِلَّا هَذَا الْيَوْمَ حِينَ قَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ: ﴿ذَرُونِي أَقْتُلْ مُوسَى﴾ ، فَأَخَذَتِ الرَّجُلَ غَضْبَةٌ لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، وَ"أَفْضَلُ الْجِهَادِ كَلِمَةُ عَدْلٍ عِنْدَ سُلْطَانٍ جَائِرٍ"، كَمَا ثَبَتَ بِذَلِكَ الْحَدِيثُ، وَلَا أَعْظَمَ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْكَلِمَةِ عِنْدَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَهِيَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَتَقْتُلُونَ رَجُلا أَنْ يَقُولَ رَبِّيَ اللَّهُ﴾ [أَيْ: لِأَجْلِ أَنْ يَقُولَ رَبِّي اللَّهُ] ، اللَّهُمَّ إِلَّا مَا رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ فِي صَحِيحِهِ حَيْثُ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ التَّيْمِيُّ، حَدَّثَنِي عُرْوَةُ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ قَالَ: قُلْتُ لِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ: أَخْبِرْنِي بِأَشَدِّ شَيْءٍ مِمَّا صَنَعَهُ الْمُشْرِكُونَ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: بَيْنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يُصَلِّي بِفِنَاءِ الْكَعْبَةِ إِذْ أَقْبَلَ عُقْبة بْنُ أَبِي مُعَيط، فَأَخَذَ بمَنْكب رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ ولَوَى ثَوْبَهُ فِي عُنُقِهِ، فَخَنَقَهُ خَنْقًا شَدِيدًا، فَأَقْبَلَ أَبُو بَكْرٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَأَخَذَ بِمَنْكِبِهِ ودَفَع عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ ثُمَّ قال: ﴿أَتَقْتُلُونَ رَجُلا أَنْ يَقُولَ رَبِّيَ اللَّهُ وَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ .

انْفَرَدَ بِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْأَوْزَاعِيِّ قَالَ: وَتَابَعَهُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا هَارُونُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ الْهَمْدَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدة عَنْ هِشَامٍ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ عُرْوَةَ-عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ أَنَّهُ سُئِل: مَا أَشَدُّ مَا رَأَيْتَ قُرَيْشًا بَلَغُوا مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ قال: مَرَّ بِهِمْ ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ فَقَالُوا لَهُ: أَنْتَ تَنْهَانَا أَنْ نَعْبُدَ مَا يَعْبُدُ آبَاؤُنَا؟ فَقَالَ: "أَنَا ذَاكَ" فَقَامُوا إِلَيْهِ، فَأَخَذُوا بِمَجَامِعِ ثِيَابِهِ، فرأيتُ أَبَا بَكْرٍ مُحْتَضِنُهُ مِنْ وَرَائِهِ، وَهُوَ يَصِيحُ بِأَعْلَى صَوْتِهِ، وَإِنَّ عَيْنَيْهِ لَيَسِيلَانِ، وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: يَا قَوْمِ، ﴿أَتَقْتُلُونَ رَجُلا أَنْ يَقُولَ رَبِّيَ اللَّهُ وَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ حَتَّى فَرَغَ مِنَ الْآيَةِ كُلِّهَا.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدَةَ، فَجَعْلَهُ مِنْ مُسْنَدِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: كَيْفَ تَقْتُلُونَ رَجُلًا لِكَوْنِهِ يَقُولُ: "رُبِّيَ اللَّهُ"، وَقَدْ أَقَامَ لَكُمُ الْبُرْهَانَ عَلَى صِدْقِ مَا جَاءَكُمْ بِهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ؟ ثُمَّ تَنزل مَعَهُمْ فِي الْمُخَاطَبَةِ فَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِنْ يَكُ كَاذِبًا فَعَلَيْهِ كَذِبُهُ وَإِنْ يَكُ صَادِقًا يُصِبْكُمْ بَعْضُ الَّذِي يَعِدُكُمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: إِذَا لَمْ يُظْهِرْ لَكُمْ صِحَّةَ مَا جَاءَكُمْ بِهِ، فَمِنَ الْعَقْلِ وَالرَّأْيِ التَّامِّ وَالْحَزَمِ أَنْ تَتْرُكُوهُ وَنَفْسَهُ، فَلَا تُؤْذُوهُ، فَإِنْ يَكُ كَاذِبًا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ سَيُجَازِيهِ عَلَى كَذِبِهِ بِالْعُقُوبَةِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، وَإِنْ يَكُ صَادِقًا وَقَدْ آذَيْتُمُوهُ يُصِبْكُمْ بَعْضُ الَّذِي يَعِدُكُمْ، فَإِنَّهُ يَتَوَعَّدُكُمْ إِنْ خَالَفْتُمُوهُ بِعَذَابٍ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، فَمِنَ الْجَائِزِ عِنْدَكُمْ أَنْ يَكُونَ صَادِقًا، فَيَنْبَغِي عَلَى هَذَا أَلَّا تَتَعَرَّضُوا لَهُ، بَلِ اتْرُكُوهُ وَقَوْمَهُ يَدْعُوهُمْ وَيَتْبَعُونَهُ.

وَهَكَذَا أَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ [تَعَالَى] عَنْ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ طَلَبَ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ وَقَوْمِهِ الْمُوَادَعَةَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ فَتَنَّا قَبْلَهُمْ قَوْمَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَجَاءَهُمْ رَسُولٌ كَرِيمٌ. أَنْ أَدُّوا إِلَيَّ عِبَادَ اللَّهِ إِنِّي لَكُمْ رَسُولٌ أَمِينٌ. وَأَنْ لا تَعْلُوا عَلَى اللَّهِ إِنِّي آتِيكُمْ بِسُلْطَانٍ مُبِينٍ. وَإِنِّي عُذْتُ بِرَبِّي وَرَبِّكُمْ أَنْ تَرْجُمُونِ. وَإِنْ لَمْ تُؤْمِنُوا لِي فَاعْتَزِلُونِ﴾ [الدُّخَانِ:١٧ -٢١] وَهَكَذَا قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِقُرَيْشٍ أَنْ يَتْرُكُوهُ يَدْعُو إِلَى اللَّهِ [تَعَالَى] عِبَادَ اللَّهِ، وَلَا يَمَسُّوهُ بِسُوءٍ، وَأَنْ يَصِلُوا مَا بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَهُمْ مِنَ الْقَرَابَةِ فِي تَرْكِ أَذِيَّتِهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ لَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا إِلا الْمَوَدَّةَ فِي الْقُرْبَى﴾ [الشُّورَى: ٢٣] أَيْ: إِلَّا أَلَّا تُؤْذُونِي فِيمَا بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَكُمْ مِنَ الْقَرَابَةِ، فَلَا تُؤْذُونِي وَتَتْرُكُوا بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَ النَّاسِ. وَعَلَى هَذَا وُقِّعَتِ الْهُدْنَةُ يَوْمَ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ، وَكَانَ فَتْحًا مُبِينًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي مَنْ هُوَ مُسْرِفٌ كَذَّابٌ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْ كَانَ هَذَا الَّذِي يَزْعُمُ أَنَّ اللَّهَ أَرْسَلَهُ إِلَيْكُمْ كَاذِبًا كَمَا تَزْعُمُونَ، لَكَانَ أَمْرُهُ بَيِّنًا، يَظْهَرُ لِكُلِّ أَحَدٍ فِي أَقْوَالِهِ وَأَفْعَالِهِ، كَانَتْ تَكُونُ فِي غَايَةِ الِاخْتِلَافِ وَالِاضْطِرَابِ، وَهَذَا نَرَى أَمْرَهُ سَدِيدًا وَمَنْهَجَهُ مُسْتَقِيمًا، وَلَوْ كَانَ مِنَ الْمُسْرِفِينَ الْكَذَّابِينَ لَمَا هَدَاهُ اللَّهُ، وَأَرْشَدَهُ إِلَى مَا تَرَوْنَ مِنِ انْتِظَامِ أَمْرِهِ وَفِعْلِهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ الْمُؤْمِنُ مُحَذِّرًا قَوْمَهُ زَوَالَ نِعْمَةِ اللَّهِ عَنْهُمْ وَحُلُولَ نِقْمَةِ اللَّهِ بِهِمْ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ لَكُمُ الْمُلْكُ الْيَوْمَ ظَاهِرِينَ فِي الأرْضِ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمْ بِهَذَا الْمُلْكِ وَالظُّهُورِ فِي الْأَرْضِ بِالْكَلِمَةِ النَّافِذَةِ وَالْجَاهِ الْعَرِيضِ، فَرَاعُوا هَذِهِ النِّعْمَةَ بِشُكْرِ اللَّهِ، وَتَصْدِيقِ رَسُولِهِ ﷺ، وَاحْذَرُوا نِقْمَةَ اللَّهِ إِنْ كَذَّبْتُمْ رَسُولَهُ، ﴿فَمَنْ يَنْصُرُنَا مِنْ بَأْسِ اللَّهِ إِنْ جَاءَنَا﴾ أَيْ: لَا تُغْنِي عَنْكُمْ هَذِهِ الْجُنُودُ وَهَذِهِ الْعَسَاكِرُ، وَلَا تَرُدُّ عَنَّا شَيْئًا مِنْ بَأْسِ اللَّهِ إِنْ أَرَادَنَا بِسُوءٍ.

﴿قَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ﴾ لِقَوْمِهِ، رَادًّا عَلَى مَا أَشَارَ بِهِ هَذَا الرَّجُلُ الصَّالِحُ الْبَارُّ الرَّاشِدُ الَّذِي كَانَ أَحَقَّ بِالْمُلْكِ مِنْ فِرْعَوْنَ: ﴿مَا أُرِيكُمْ إِلا مَا أَرَى﴾ أَيْ: مَا أَقُولُ لَكُمْ وَأُشِيرُ عَلَيْكُمْ إِلَّا مَا أَرَاهُ لِنَفْسِي وَقَدْ كَذَبَ فِرْعَوْنُ، فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ يَتَحَقَّقُ صِدْقَ مُوسَى فِيمَا جَاءَ بِهِ مِنَ الرِّسَالَةِ ﴿قَالَ لَقَدْ عَلِمْتَ مَا أَنزلَ هَؤُلاءِ إِلا رَبُّ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ بَصَائِرَ﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ:١٠٢] ، وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَجَحَدُوا بِهَا وَاسْتَيْقَنَتْهَا أَنْفُسُهُمْ ظُلْمًا وَعُلُوًّا﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ١٤] .

فَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿مَا أُرِيكُمْ إِلا مَا أَرَى﴾ كَذَبَ فِيهِ وَافْتَرَى، وَخَانَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ وَرَعِيَّتَهُ، فَغَشَّهُمْ وَمَا نَصَحَهُمْ وَكَذَا قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا أَهْدِيكُمْ إِلا سَبِيلَ الرَّشَادِ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا أَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَّا إِلَى طَرِيقِ الْحَقِّ وَالصِّدْقِ وَالرُّشْدِ وَقَدْ كَذَبَ أَيْضًا فِي ذَلِكَ، وَإِنْ كَانَ قَوْمُهُ قَدْ أَطَاعُوهُ وَاتَّبَعُوهُ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَاتَّبَعُوا أَمْرَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَمَا أَمْرُ فِرْعَوْنَ بِرَشِيدٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٩٧] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَضَلَّ فِرْعَوْنُ قَوْمَهُ وَمَا هَدَى﴾ [طَهَ: ٧٩] ، وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ: "مَا مِنْ إِمَامٍ يَمُوتُ يَوْمَ يَمُوتُ وَهُوَ غَاشٌّ لِرَعِيَّتِهِ، إِلَّا لَمْ يَرح رَائِحَةَ الْجَنَّةِ، وَإِنَّ رِيحَهَا لِيُوجَدُ مِنْ مَسِيرَةِ خَمْسِمِائَةِ عَامٍ" .

---

## 40:30-35 — verses 30-35 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is an account from Allah, mighty and majestic, about this righteous man, the believer of the family of Pharaoh: that he warned his people of the punishment of Allah in this world and the next, saying: {O my people, I fear for you something like the day of the confederates}, meaning those who denied the messengers of Allah in ancient times, such as the people of Nuh, 'Ad and Thamud, and those nations of deniers who came after them, how the punishment of Allah befell them, and no one could ward it off from them, nor could anyone repel it from them.

{And Allah does not intend injustice for His servants}, meaning: Allah only destroyed them because of their sins, their denial of His messengers, and their opposition to His command. So He carried out His decree against them. Then he said: {And O my people, I fear for you the Day of Calling}, meaning the Day of Resurrection. It was named thus, some of them said, because it comes in the hadith of the Trumpet that when the earth is shaken and splits from one edge to another, and surges and quakes, people, seeing that, will flee, calling out to one another.

Others among them, including al-Dahhak, said: rather, that is when Hell is brought forth, and people flee in terror, but the angels intercept them and turn them back to the place of the gathering. This is the meaning of His statement: {and the angels will be at its edges} [al-Haqqah: 17], and His statement: {O company of jinn and men, if you are able to pass beyond the regions of the heavens and the earth, then pass. You will not pass except by authority} [al-Rahman: 33].

It has been reported from Ibn 'Abbas, al-Hasan, and al-Dahhak that they read it as "Yawm al-Tanaadd" with the doubling of the dal, from the verb "nadda," said of a camel: when it bolts and runs off.

It is also said that this is because at the Balance there is an angel, and when he weighs the deed of a servant and it is heavy, he calls out at the top of his voice: Indeed, so-and-so son of so-and-so has attained happiness, a happiness after which he will never be wretched. And if his deed is light, he calls out: Indeed, so-and-so son of so-and-so has become wretched.

Qatadah said: every people will be called by their deeds. The people of Paradise will be called "people of Paradise," and the people of the Fire will be called "people of the Fire."

It is also said that it was named thus because of the calling out of the people of Paradise to the people of the Fire: {We have found what our Lord promised us to be true. Have you found what your Lord promised to be true? They will say: Yes} [al-A'raf: 44]. And the calling out of the people of the Fire to the people of Paradise: {Pour upon us some water or of what Allah has provided you. They will say: Allah has forbidden both to the disbelievers} [al-A'raf: 50]. And also because of the calling out of the People of the Heights to the people of Paradise and the people of the Fire, as is mentioned in Surat al-A'raf.

Al-Baghawi and others chose the view that it was named thus for all of these reasons together. This is a good and sound view, and Allah knows best.

His statement: {The day you will turn your backs and flee}, meaning going away in flight, {No! There is no refuge. To your Lord that Day is the place of settlement} [al-Qiyamah: 11-12]. And for this reason He said: {You will have no protector from Allah}, meaning: you will have no one to prevent you from Allah's punishment and torment. {And whoever Allah sends astray, for him there is no guide}, meaning: whoever Allah has sent astray has no guide other than Him.

His statement: {And Yusuf had already come to you before with clear proofs}, meaning the people of Egypt: Allah had sent among them a messenger before Musa, namely Yusuf (peace be upon him), who was the vizier ('aziz) of the people of Egypt, and was a messenger calling his people, the Copts, to Allah. Yet they only obeyed him at that time merely because of his position as vizier and his worldly standing. For this reason He said: {But you remained in doubt about what he brought you, until when he died, you said: Allah will never send a messenger after him}, meaning: you despaired, and said, presuming: {Allah will never send a messenger after him}, and that was because of their disbelief and their denial. {Thus does Allah send astray whoever is a transgressor and a doubter}, meaning: like your own condition now.

Then He said: {Those who dispute concerning the signs of Allah without any authority having come to them}, meaning: those who repel truth with falsehood, and dispute against proofs without any evidence or argument from Allah with them. Allah detests this with the utmost hatred. For this reason He, exalted, said: {It is greatly hateful in the sight of Allah and in the sight of those who believe}, meaning: the believers also hate whoever has this characteristic. For whoever has this characteristic, Allah seals his heart, so that after that he recognizes no good and denounces no evil. For this reason He said: {Thus does Allah seal up every heart of an arrogant}, meaning: arrogant against following the truth, {tyrant}.

Ibn Abi Hatim reported from 'Ikrimah, and it was also related from al-Sha'bi, that they both said: a person is not considered a tyrant (jabbar) until he has killed two souls.

Abu 'Imran al-Jawni and Qatadah said: the sign of tyrants is killing without right.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا إِخْبَارٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، عَنْ هَذَا الرَّجُلِ الصَّالِحِ، مُؤْمِنِ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ: أَنَّهُ حَذَّرَ قَوْمَهُ بَأْسَ اللَّهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ إِنِّي أَخَافُ عَلَيْكُمْ مِثْلَ يَوْمِ الأحْزَابِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ كَذَّبُوا رُسُلَ اللَّهِ فِي قَدِيمِ الدَّهْرِ، كَقَوْمِ نُوحٍ وَعَادٍ وَثَمُودَ، وَالَّذِينَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ، كَيْفَ حَلَّ بِهِمْ بَأْسُ اللَّهِ، وَمَا رَدَّهُ عَنْهُمْ رَادٌّ، وَلَا صَدَّهُ عنهم صاد.

﴿وَمَا اللَّهُ يُرِيدُ ظُلْمًا لِلْعِبَادِ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا أَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ، وَتَكْذِيبِهِمْ رُسُلَهُ، وَمُخَالَفَتِهِمْ أَمْرَهُ. فَأَنْفَذَ فِيهِمْ قَدَرَهُ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿وَيَا قَوْمِ إِنِّي أَخَافُ عَلَيْكُمْ يَوْمَ التَّنَادِ﴾ يَعْنِي: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَسُمِّيَ بِذَلِكَ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: لَمَّا جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثِ الصُّورِ: إِنَّ الْأَرْضَ إِذَا زُلْزِلَتْ وَانْشَقَّتْ مِنْ قُطْرٍ إِلَى قُطْرٍ، وَمَاجَتْ وَارْتَجَّتْ، فَنَظَرَ النَّاسُ إِلَى ذَلِكَ ذَهَبُوا هَارِبِينَ يُنَادِي بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ مِنْهُمُ الضَّحَّاكُ: بَلْ ذَلِكَ إِذَا جِيءَ بِجَهَنَّمَ، ذَهَبَ النَّاسُ هِرَابا ، فَتَتَلَقَّاهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ فَتَرُدُّهُمْ إِلَى مَقَامِ الْمَحْشَرِ، وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَالْمَلَكُ عَلَى أَرْجَائِهَا﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١٧] ، وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿يَا مَعْشَرَ الْجِنِّ وَالإنْسِ إِنِ اسْتَطَعْتُمْ أَنْ تَنْفُذُوا مِنْ أَقْطَارِ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ فَانْفُذُوا لَا تَنْفُذُونَ إِلا بِسُلْطَانٍ﴾ [الرَّحْمَنِ:٣٣] .

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ: أَنَّهُمْ قَرَؤُوا: "يَوْمَ التَّنَادِّ" بِتَشْدِيدِ الدَّالِّ مِنْ نَدَّ الْبَعِيرُ: إِذَا شَرَدَ وَذَهَبَ.

وَقِيلَ: لِأَنَّ الْمِيزَانَ عِنْدَهُ مَلَكٌ، وَإِذَا وَزَنَ عَمَلَ الْعَبْدِ فَرَجَحَ نَادَى بِأَعْلَى صَوْتِهِ: أَلَا قَدْ سَعِدَ فَلَانُ بْنُ فُلَانٌ سَعَادَةً لَا يَشْقَى بَعْدَهَا أَبَدًا. وَإِنْ خَفَّ عَمَلُهُ نَادَى: أَلَا قَدْ شَقِيَ فَلَانُ بْنُ فُلَانٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: يُنَادَى كُلُّ قَوْمٍ بِأَعْمَالِهِمْ: يُنَادَى أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ، وَأَهْلُ النَّارِ أَهْلَ النَّارِ.

وَقِيلَ: سُمِّيَ بِذَلِكَ لِمُنَادَاةِ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ أَهْلَ النَّارِ: ﴿أَنْ قَدْ وَجَدْنَا مَا وَعَدَنَا رَبُّنَا حَقًّا فَهَلْ وَجَدْتُمْ مَا وَعَدَ رَبُّكُمْ حَقًّا قَالُوا نَعَمْ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٤٤] . وَمُنَادَاةُ أَهْلِ النَّارِ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ: ﴿أَنْ أَفِيضُوا عَلَيْنَا مِنَ الْمَاءِ أَوْ مِمَّا رَزَقَكُمُ اللَّهُ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ حَرَّمَهُمَا عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٥٠] ، وَلِمُنَادَاةِ أَصْحَابِ الْأَعْرَافِ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ وَأَهْلَ النَّارِ، كَمَا هُوَ مَذْكُورٌ فِي سُورَةِ الْأَعْرَافِ.

وَاخْتَارَ الْبَغَوِيُّ وَغَيْرُهُ: أَنَّهُ سُمِّيَ بِذَلِكَ لِمَجْمُوعِ ذَلِكَ. وَهُوَ قَوْلٌ حَسَنٌ جَيِّدٌ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَوْمَ تُوَلُّونَ مُدْبِرِينَ﴾ أَيْ: ذَاهِبِينَ هَارِبِينَ، ﴿كَلا لَا وَزَرَ. إِلَى رَبِّكَ يَوْمَئِذٍ الْمُسْتَقَرُّ﴾ [الْقِيَامَةِ: ١١، ١٢] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَا لَكُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنْ عَاصِمٍ﴾ أَيْ: مَا لَكُمْ مَانِعٌ يَمْنَعُكُمْ مِنْ بَأْسِ اللَّهِ وَعَذَابِهِ، ﴿وَمَنْ يُضْلِلِ اللَّهُ فَمَا لَهُ مِنْ هَادٍ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ أَضَلَّهُ [اللَّهُ] فَلَا هَادِيَ لَهُ غَيْرُهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ جَاءَكُمْ يُوسُفُ مِنْ قَبْلُ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ﴾ يَعْنِي: أَهْلَ مِصْرَ، قَدْ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ فِيهِمْ رَسُولًا مِنْ قَبْلِ مُوسَى، وَهُوَ يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَانَ عَزِيزَ أَهْلِ مِصْرَ، وَكَانَ رَسُولًا يَدْعُو إِلَى اللَّهِ أُمَّتَهُ الْقِبْطَ، فَمَا أَطَاعُوهُ تِلْكَ السَّاعَةَ إِلَّا لِمُجَرَّدِ الْوِزَارَةِ وَالْجَاهِ الدُّنْيَوِيِّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَمَا زِلْتُمْ فِي شَكٍّ مِمَّا جَاءَكُمْ بِهِ حَتَّى إِذَا هَلَكَ قُلْتُمْ لَنْ يَبْعَثَ اللَّهُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ رَسُولا﴾ أَيْ: يَئِسْتُمْ فَقُلْتُمْ طَامِعِينَ: ﴿لَنْ يَبْعَثَ اللَّهُ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ رَسُولا﴾ وَذَلِكَ لِكُفْرِهِمْ وَتَكْذِيبِهِمْ ﴿كَذَلِكَ يُضِلُّ اللَّهُ مَنْ هُوَ مُسْرِفٌ مُرْتَابٌ﴾ أي: كحالكم هذا.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿الَّذِينَ يُجَادِلُونَ فِي آيَاتِ اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ سُلْطَانٍ أَتَاهُمْ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِينَ يَدْفَعُونَ الْحَقَّ بِالْبَاطِلِ، وَيُجَادِلُونَ الْحُجَجَ بِغَيْرِ دَلِيلٍ وَحُجَّةٍ مَعَهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَمْقُتُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ أَشَدَّ الْمَقْتِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿كَبُرَ مَقْتًا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَعِنْدَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا﴾ أَيْ: وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ أَيْضًا يُبغضُون مَنْ تَكُونُ هَذِهِ صِفَتَهُ، فَإِنَّ مَنْ كَانَتْ هَذِهِ صِفَتَهُ، يَطْبَعُ اللَّهُ عَلَى قَلْبِهِ، فَلَا يَعْرِفُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ مَعْرُوفًا، وَلَا يُنْكِرُ مُنْكَرًا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ يَطْبَعُ اللَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ قَلْبِ مُتَكَبِّرٍ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى اتِّبَاعِ الْحَقِّ ﴿جَبَّارٍ﴾ .

وَرَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ -وَحُكِيَ عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ-أَنَّهُمَا قَالَا لَا يَكُونُ الْإِنْسَانُ جَبَّارًا حَتَّى يَقْتُلَ نَفْسَيْنِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو عِمْرَانَ الْجَوْنِيُّ وَقَتَادَةُ: آيَةُ الْجَبَابِرَةِ الْقَتْلُ بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ.

---

## 40:36-37 — verses 36-37 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, informing about Pharaoh, his tyranny, his rebellion, and his fabrication in denying Musa (peace be upon him), that he ordered his minister Haman to build for him a sarh, which is the high, towering, lofty palace. Its construction was made from baked brick fired from clay, as He said: {So kindle for me, O Haman, a fire upon the clay, and make for me a sarh} [al-Qasas: 38]. For this reason Ibrahim al-Nakha'i said: They used to dislike building with baked brick, and using it in their graves. Reported by Ibn Abi Hatim.

As for His saying: {that perhaps I may reach the ways, the ways of the heavens}, Sa'id ibn Jubayr and Abu Salih said: the doors of the heavens. And it was said: the paths of the heavens. {And look upon the God of Musa, for indeed I think he is a liar}. This is part of his disbelief and his rebellion, that he denied Musa in the matter of Allah, Mighty and Majestic, having sent him to him. Allah the Almighty said: {Thus was the evil of his deed made fair-seeming to Pharaoh, and he was averted from the path}, meaning: by this scheme of his, through which he wanted to give the people the false impression that he was doing something that would lead to the exposure of Musa's falsehood (peace be upon him). For this reason the Almighty said: {And the plot of Pharaoh was doomed only to failure}. Ibn Abbas [may Allah be pleased with both of them] and Mujahid said: meaning, only in loss.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنْ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَعُتُوِّهُ، وَتَمَرُّدِهِ، وَافْتِرَائِهِ فِي تَكْذِيبِهِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُ أَمَرَ وَزِيرَهُ هَامَانَ أَنْ يَبْنِيَ لَهُ صَرْحًا، وَهُوَ: الْقَصْرُ الْعَالِي الْمُنِيفُ الشَّاهِقُ. وَكَانَ اتِّخَاذُهُ مِنَ الْآجُرِّ الْمَضْرُوبِ مِنَ الطِّينِ الْمَشْوِيِّ، كَمَا قال: ﴿فَأَوْقِدْ لِي يَاهَامَانُ عَلَى الطِّينِ فَاجْعَلْ لِي صَرْحًا﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٣٨] ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيُّ: كَانُوا يَكْرَهُونَ الْبِنَاءَ بِالْآجُرِّ، وَأَنْ يَجْعَلُوهُ فِي قُبُورِهِمْ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَعَلِّي أَبْلُغُ الأسْبَابَ أَسْبَابَ السَّمَوَاتِ﴾ قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَأَبُو صَالِحٍ: أَبْوَابَ السموات. وقيل: طرق السَّمَوَاتِ ﴿فَأَطَّلِعَ إِلَى إِلَهِ مُوسَى وَإِنِّي لأظُنُّهُ كَاذِبًا﴾ ، وَهَذَا مِنْ كُفْرِهِ وَتَمَرُّدِهِ، أَنَّهُ كَذَّبَ مُوسَى فِي أَنَّ اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، أَرْسَلَهُ إِلَيْهِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَذَلِكَ زُيِّنَ لِفِرْعَوْنَ سُوءُ عَمَلِهِ وَصُدَّ عَنِ السَّبِيلِ﴾ أَيْ: بِصَنِيعِهِ هَذَا الَّذِي أَرَادَ أَنْ يُوهِمَ بِهِ الرَّعِيَّةَ أَنَّهُ يَعْمَلُ شَيْئًا يَتَوَصَّلُ بِهِ إِلَى تَكْذِيبِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا كَيْدُ فِرْعَوْنَ إِلا فِي تَبَابٍ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ [رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا] ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي إِلَّا فِي خَسَارٍ.

---

## 40:38-40 — verses 38-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The believer said to his people, those who had rebelled, transgressed, preferred the worldly life, and forgotten the Almighty on High: {O my people, follow me and I will guide you to the way of right conduct}.

Not as Pharaoh lied in his saying: {and I only guide you to the way of right conduct}.

Then he made them view with disdain the worldly life which they had preferred over the Hereafter, and which had turned them away from believing in the Messenger of Allah, Musa (peace be upon him). So he said: {O my people, this worldly life is but a passing enjoyment}, meaning it is little, fleeting, and perishing, soon to go away, disappear, and vanish, {while the Hereafter is truly the abode of settlement}, meaning the abode that has no passing away, no removal from it, and no departure from it to another. Rather, it is either everlasting bliss or everlasting torment. For this reason He said: {Whoever does an evil deed will not be recompensed except with its like}, meaning a single like recompense, {but whoever does righteous deeds, whether male or female, while being a believer, those will enter Paradise, provided for therein without account}, meaning it is not measured out by a fixed recompense, but rather Allah rewards him with abundant reward that has no end and no exhaustion.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ الْمُؤْمِنُ لِقَوْمِهِ مِمَّنْ تَمَرَّدَ وَطَغَى وَآثَرَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا، وَنَسِيَ الْجَبَّارَ الْأَعْلَى، فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ اتَّبِعُونِ أَهْدِكُمْ سَبِيلَ الرَّشَادِ﴾

لَا كَمَا كَذَبَ فِرْعَوْنُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا أَهْدِيكُمْ إِلا سَبِيلَ الرَّشَادِ﴾ .

ثُمَّ زَهَّدَهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا الَّتِي [قَدْ] آثَرُوهَا عَلَى الْأُخْرَى، وَصَدَّتْهُمْ عَنِ التَّصْدِيقِ بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ مُوسَى [ﷺ] ، فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا قَوْمِ إِنَّمَا هَذِهِ الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا مَتَاعٌ﴾ أَيْ: قَلِيلَةٌ زَائِلَةٌ فَانِيَةٌ عَنْ قَرِيبٍ تَذْهَبُ [وَتَزُولُ] وَتَضْمَحِلُّ، ﴿وَإِنَّ الآخِرَةَ هِيَ دَارُ الْقَرَارِ﴾ أَيِ: الدَّارُ الَّتِي لَا زَوَالَ لَهَا، وَلَا انْتِقَالَ مِنْهَا وَلَا ظَعْنَ عَنْهَا إِلَى غَيْرِهَا، بَلْ إِمَّا نَعِيمٌ وَإِمَّا جَحِيمٌ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ ﴿مَنْ عَمِلَ سَيِّئَةً فَلا يُجْزَى إِلا مِثْلَهَا﴾ أَيْ: وَاحِدَةً مِثْلَهَا ﴿وَمَنْ عَمِلَ صَالِحًا مِنْ ذَكَرٍ أَوْ أُنْثَى وَهُوَ مُؤْمِنٌ فَأُولَئِكَ يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ يُرْزَقُونَ فِيهَا بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَتَقَدَّرُ بِجَزَاءٍ بَلْ يُثِيبُهُ اللَّهُ، ثَوَابًا كَثِيرًا لَا انْقِضَاءَ لَهُ وَلَا نفاد.

---

## 40:41-46 — verses 41-46 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The believer says to them: What is wrong with me, that I call you to salvation, which is worshiping God alone with no partner and affirming the truth of His Messenger whom He has sent, {while you call me to the Fire. You call me to disbelieve in God and to associate with Him that of which I have no knowledge}, meaning: ignorance without any proof, {while I call you to the Almighty, the Ever-Forgiving}, meaning: He, in His might and majesty, forgives the sin of whoever turns to Him in repentance. {There is no doubt that what you call me to} means: truly.

Al-Suddi and Ibn Jarir said: the meaning of His saying {la jarama (there is no doubt)} is "truly."

Al-Dahhak said: {la jarama} means "no falsehood."

Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas: {la jarama} means: indeed, that which you call me to, namely the idols and rivals, {has no calling in this world or in the Hereafter}.

Mujahid said: the idol is nothing.

Qatadah said: it means the idol neither benefits nor harms.

Al-Suddi said: it does not answer the one who calls upon it, neither in this world nor in the Hereafter.

This is like His saying, Exalted is He: {And who is more astray than one who calls upon, besides God, that which cannot answer him until the Day of Resurrection, and who are unaware of their calling. And when mankind is gathered, they will be enemies to them and will deny their worship} [al-Ahqaf: 5, 6], and {If you call upon them, they do not hear your call, and if they heard, they would not respond to you} [Fatir: 14].

* *

His saying, {and that our return is to God}, means: in the Hereafter, where He will repay each according to his deed. That is why He said: {and that the transgressors are the companions of the Fire}, meaning: abiding therein eternally because of their transgression, which is their associating partners with God.

{So you will remember what I say to you}, means: you will come to know the truth of what I commanded you and forbade you, and the counsel I gave you and made clear to you, and you will remember it, and you will regret it when regret will not benefit you. {And I entrust my affair to God}, meaning: I rely upon God and seek His help, and I sever ties with you and distance myself from you. {Indeed, God is all-seeing of His servants}, meaning: He sees them fully, so He guides whoever deserves guidance and leads astray whoever deserves to be led astray, and His is the conclusive proof, the complete wisdom, and the decree that is carried out.

* *

His saying, [Exalted is He]: {So God protected him from the evils of what they plotted}, meaning: in this world and in the Hereafter. As for this world, God saved him along with Moses (peace be upon him), and as for the Hereafter, it was by way of Paradise. {And the people of Pharaoh were overtaken by the worst punishment}, which is: drowning in the sea, then being transferred from it to the Blazing Fire. For their souls are exposed to the Fire morning and evening until the establishment of the Hour, and when the Day of Resurrection comes, their souls and bodies will be gathered together in the Fire. That is why He said: {And on the Day the Hour is established: admit the people of Pharaoh into the severest punishment}, meaning: the most painful and greatest in retribution. This verse is a major foundation used by the people of the Sunnah as evidence for the punishment of the barzakh (intermediate state) in the graves, namely His saying: {The Fire, they are exposed to it morning and evening}.

But there is a question here, which is that there is no doubt that this verse is Meccan, and yet it has been used as evidence for the punishment of the grave in the barzakh. Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Hashim, that is Ibn al-Qasim Abu al-Nadr, told us, Ishaq ibn Sa'id, that is Ibn Amr ibn Sa'id ibn al-'As, told us, Sa'id, meaning his father, told us, from Aishah: that a Jewish woman used to serve her, and whenever Aishah did her any kindness the Jewish woman would say to her, "May God protect you from the punishment of the grave." She said: The Messenger of God ﷺ came in to me, and I said: O Messenger of God, is there punishment in the grave before the Day of Resurrection? He said: "No, and why do you ask that?" She said: This Jewish woman, whenever we do her any kindness, says: "May God protect you from the punishment of the grave." He said: "The Jews have lied. And they are more untruthful before God. There is no punishment before the Day of Resurrection." Then he remained however long God willed him to remain, and one day he went out at midday wrapped in his garment, his eyes reddened, calling out at the top of his voice: "The grave is like the darkest pieces of the night. O people, if you knew what I know, you would weep much and laugh little. O people, seek refuge in God from the punishment of the grave, for indeed the punishment of the grave is real."

This is a sound chain meeting the standard of al-Bukhari and Muslim, though neither of them recorded it.

Ahmad also narrated: [chain] Yazid told us, Sufyan told us, from al-Zuhri, from Urwah, from Aishah, who said: A Jewish woman asked her for something and she gave it to her, and the woman said to her: "May God protect you from the punishment of the grave." Aishah found this objectionable, and when she saw the Messenger of God ﷺ she mentioned it to him, and he said: "No." Aishah said: Then afterward the Messenger of God ﷺ said to us: "It has been revealed to me that you will be tested in your graves."

This too meets the standard of both Bukhari and Muslim.

So it may be asked: how can this be reconciled with the fact that the verse is Meccan, while it contains evidence for the punishment of the barzakh? The answer is: the verse indicates the exposure of the souls to the Fire morning and evening in the barzakh, but it contains no indication that this suffering is connected to their bodies in the graves, since it may be that this is specific to the soul alone. As for this occurring to the body and its suffering because of it, only the Sunnah, in the trustworthy hadiths to be mentioned, indicates that.

It may also be said that this verse indicates only the punishment of the disbelievers in the barzakh, and it does not necessarily follow from this that the believer is punished in his grave for a sin. Among what indicates this is what Imam Ahmad narrated:

[chain] Uthman ibn Umar told us, Yunus told us, from al-Zuhri, from Urwah, from Aishah, may God be pleased with her: that the Messenger of God ﷺ came in to her while a Jewish woman was with her, and she was saying: "Are you aware that you will be tested in your graves?" The Messenger of God ﷺ was alarmed and said: "It is only the Jews who are tested." Aishah said: We remained for some nights, then the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Are you aware that it has been revealed to me that you will be tested in the graves?" Aishah said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ afterward seeking refuge from the punishment of the grave.

Muslim narrated it likewise, from Harun ibn Sa'id and Harmalah, both from Ibn Wahb, from Yunus ibn Yazid al-Ayli, from al-Zuhri, with the same content.

It may also be said: this verse indicates the punishment of the souls in the barzakh, and it does not necessarily follow that this is connected to the bodies in their graves. So when he ﷺ was informed of this specifically by revelation, he sought refuge from it. And God, Glorified and Exalted, knows best.

Al-Bukhari narrated, from the hadith of Shu'bah, from Ash'ath ibn Abi al-Sha'tha, from his father, from Masruq, from Aishah, may God be pleased with her: that a Jewish woman came in to her and said: "May God protect you from the punishment of the grave." So Aishah asked the Messenger of God ﷺ about the punishment of the grave, and he said: "Yes, the punishment of the grave is real." Aishah said: I never afterward saw the Messenger of God ﷺ pray a prayer without seeking refuge from the punishment of the grave.

This indicates that he was quick to confirm the truth of what the Jewish woman said in this report, and affirmed it. But in the earlier reports, he denied it until revelation came to him. Perhaps these are two separate incidents, and God knows best. The hadiths about the punishment of the grave are extremely numerous.

Qatadah said regarding His saying {morning and evening}: morning and evening, for as long as this world remains, it will be said to them: "O people of Pharaoh, these are your abodes," as a rebuke, a punishment, and a humiliation for them.

Ibn Zayd said: they are in it today, taken out morning and evening, until the Hour is established.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Sa'id told us, al-Muharibi told us, Layth told us, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Tharwan, from Hudhayl, from Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, may God be pleased with him, who said: The souls of the martyrs are in the bodies of green birds that roam freely in Paradise wherever they wish, and the souls of the children of the believers are in the bodies of sparrows that roam freely in Paradise wherever they wish, taking refuge in lamps hung from the Throne, and the souls of the people of Pharaoh are in the bodies of black birds that go morning and evening over Hellfire, and that is their exposure.

Al-Thawri narrated it from Abu Qays, from al-Huzayl ibn Shurahbil, as his own statement about the souls of the people of Pharaoh. Al-Suddi said likewise.

In the hadith of the Night Journey, in the narration of Abu Harun al-Abdi, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may God be pleased with him, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, it states: "Then I was taken to a great multitude of God's creation, men, each of them with a belly like a huge house, shackled upon the path of the people of Pharaoh, and the people of Pharaoh are exposed to the Fire morning and evening."

{And on the Day when the Hour arrives: Admit the family of Pharaoh into the severest punishment} and the family of Pharaoh are like branded camels, striking against stones and trees, without comprehension.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ali ibn al-Husayn told us, Zayd ibn Akhram told us, Amir ibn Mudrik al-Harithi told us, Utbah, meaning Ibn Yaqzan, told us, from Qays ibn Muslim, from Tariq, from Shihab, from Ibn Mas'ud, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "No doer of good among Muslims or disbelievers does good except that Allah rewards him for it." He said: We asked, "O Messenger of Allah, what is the reward of the disbeliever?" He said: "If he maintained ties of kinship, or gave charity, or did a good deed, Allah rewards him with wealth, children, health, and things like that." We said, "Then what is his reward in the Hereafter?" He said: "A punishment lighter than the punishment," and he recited: {Admit the family of Pharaoh into the severest punishment}. Al-Bazzar related it in his Musnad from Zayd ibn Akhram, then said: We do not know of any chain for it other than this one.

Ibn Jarir said: Abd al-Karim ibn Abi Umayr told us, Hammad ibn Muhammad al-Fazari al-Balkhi told us, he said: I heard al-Awza'i, when a man asked him and said: May Allah have mercy on you. We have seen birds coming out of the sea, heading toward the west, white, in successive flocks, whose number none knows but Allah, mighty and majestic is He. Then when evening comes, the same number return, black. He said: Have you noticed that? He said: Yes. He said: Those birds carry in their crops the souls of the family of Pharaoh. They are presented to the Fire morning and evening, then return to their nests with their feathers burnt and turned black. Then white feathers grow on them during the night, and the black ones fall away. Then they go out to the Fire again, morning and evening, then return to their nests. That is their condition in this world. Then when the Day of Resurrection comes, Allah, Exalted is He, will say: {Admit the family of Pharaoh into the severest punishment}. He said: And they used to say that they numbered six hundred thousand fighting men.

Imam Ahmad said: Ishaq told us, Malik informed us, from Nafi', from Ibn Umar, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When one of you dies, his seat is shown to him morning and evening. If he is among the people of Paradise, then from the people of Paradise, and if he is among the people of the Fire, then from the people of the Fire. Then it is said: This is your seat until Allah, mighty and majestic is He, raises you up on the Day of Resurrection."

Both of them (al-Bukhari and Muslim) recorded it in the two Sahihs from the hadith of Malik, with this chain.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ لَهُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُ: مَا بَالِي أَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَى النَّجَاةِ، وَهِيَ عِبَادَةُ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ وَتَصْدِيقُ رَسُولِهِ الَّذِي بَعَثَهُ ﴿وَتَدْعُونَنِي إِلَى النَّارِ. تَدْعُونَنِي لأكْفُرَ بِاللَّهِ وَأُشْرِكَ بِهِ مَا لَيْسَ لِي بِهِ عِلْمٌ﴾ أَيْ: جَهْلٌ بِلَا دَلِيلٍ ﴿وَأَنَا أَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَى الْعَزِيزِ الْغَفَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ فِي عِزَّتِهِ وَكِبْرِيَائِهِ يَغْفِرُ ذَنْبَ مَنْ تَابَ إِلَيْهِ، ﴿لَا جَرَمَ أَنَّمَا تَدْعُونَنِي إِلَيْهِ﴾ يَقُولُ: حَقًّا.

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: مَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَا جَرَمَ﴾ حَقًّا.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: ﴿لَا جَرَمَ﴾ لَا كَذِبَ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿لَا جَرَمَ﴾ يَقُولُ: بَلَى، إِنَّ الَّذِي تَدْعُونَنِي إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَنْدَادِ ﴿لَيْسَ لَهُ دَعْوَةٌ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَلا فِي الآخِرَةِ﴾

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْوَثَنُ لَيْسَ بِشَيْءٍ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: يَعْنِي الْوَثَنَ لَا يَنْفَعُ وَلَا يَضُرُّ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: لَا يُجِيبُ دَاعِيَهُ، لَا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَلَا فِي الْآخِرَةِ.

وَهَذَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَنْ أَضَلُّ مِمَّنْ يَدْعُو مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَنْ لَا يَسْتَجِيبُ لَهُ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَهُمْ عَنْ دُعَائِهِمْ غَافِلُونَ. وَإِذَا حُشِرَ النَّاسُ كَانُوا لَهُمْ أَعْدَاءً وَكَانُوا بِعِبَادَتِهِمْ كَافِرِينَ﴾ [الْأَحْقَافِ: ٥، ٦] ، ﴿إِنْ تَدْعُوهُمْ لَا يَسْمَعُوا دُعَاءَكُمْ وَلَوْ سَمِعُوا مَا اسْتَجَابُوا لَكُمْ﴾ [فاطر: ١٤] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأَنَّ مَرَدَّنَا إِلَى اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، فَيُجَازِي كُلًّا بِعَمَلِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَأَنَّ الْمُسْرِفِينَ هُمْ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا بِإِسْرَافِهِمْ، وَهُوَ شِرْكُهُمْ بِاللَّهِ.

﴿فَسَتَذْكُرُونَ مَا أَقُولُ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: سَوْفَ تَعْلَمُونَ صِدْقَ مَا أَمَرْتُكُمْ بِهِ وَنَهَيْتُكُمْ عَنْهُ، وَنَصَحْتُكُمْ وَوَضَّحْتُ لَكُمْ، وَتَتَذَكَّرُونَهُ، وَتَنْدَمُونَ حَيْثُ لَا يَنْفَعُكُمُ النَّدَمُ، ﴿وَأُفَوِّضُ أَمْرِي إِلَى اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: وَأَتَوَكَّلُ عَلَى اللَّهِ وَأَسْتَعِينُهُ، وَأُقَاطِعُكُمْ وَأُبَاعِدُكُمْ، ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ بَصِيرٌ بِالْعِبَادِ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ بَصِيرٌ بِهِمْ، فَيَهْدِي مَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْهِدَايَةَ، وَيُضِلُّ مَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْإِضْلَالَ، وَلَهُ الْحُجَّةُ الْبَالِغَةُ، وَالْحِكْمَةُ التَّامَّةُ، وَالْقَدَرُ النَّافِذُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ [تَعَالَى] : ﴿فَوَقَاهُ اللَّهُ سَيِّئَاتِ مَا مَكَرُوا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، أَمَّا فِي الدُّنْيَا فَنَجَّاهُ اللَّهُ مَعَ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَأَمَّا فِي الْآخِرَةِ فَبِالْجَنَّةِ ﴿وَحَاقَ بِآلِ فِرْعَوْنَ سُوءُ الْعَذَابِ﴾ وَهُوَ: الْغَرَقُ فِي الْيَمِّ، ثُمَّ النَّقْلَةُ مِنْهُ إِلَى الْجَحِيمِ. فَإِنَّ أَرْوَاحَهُمْ تُعْرَضُ عَلَى النَّارِ صَبَاحًا وَمَسَاءً إِلَى قِيَامِ السَّاعَةِ، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ اجْتَمَعَتْ أَرْوَاحُهُمْ وَأَجْسَادُهُمْ فِي النَّارِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ أَدْخِلُوا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ أَشَدَّ الْعَذَابِ﴾ أَيْ: أَشَدَّهُ أَلَمًا وَأَعْظَمَهُ نَكَالًا. وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ أَصْلٌ كَبِيرٌ فِي اسْتِدْلَالِ أَهْلِ السُّنَّةِ عَلَى عَذَابِ الْبَرْزَخِ فِي الْقُبُورِ، وَهِيَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿النَّارُ يُعْرَضُونَ عَلَيْهَا غُدُوًّا وَعَشِيًّا﴾ .

وَلَكِنَّ هَاهُنَا سُؤَالٌ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ لَا شَكَّ أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ مَكِّيَّةٌ، وَقَدِ اسْتَدَلُّوا بِهَا عَلَى عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ فِي الْبَرْزَخِ، وَقَدْ قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمٌ -هُوَ ابْنُ الْقَاسِمِ أَبُو النَّضْرِ-حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ بْنُ سَعِيدٍ -هُوَ ابْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْعَاصِ-حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدٌ -يَعْنِي أَبَاهُ-عَنْ عَائِشَةَ؛ أَنَّ يَهُودِيَّةً كَانَتْ تَخْدُمُهَا فَلَا تَصْنَعُ عَائِشَةُ إِلَيْهَا شَيْئًا مِنَ الْمَعْرُوفِ إِلَّا قَالَتْ لَهَا الْيَهُودِيَّةُ: وَقَاكِ اللَّهُ عَذَابَ الْقَبْرِ. قَالَتْ: فَدَخَلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَلَيَّ فَقُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَلْ لِلْقَبْرِ عَذَابٌ قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ؟ قَالَ: "لَا وَعَمَّ ذَلِكَ؟ " قَالَتْ: هَذِهِ الْيَهُودِيَّةُ، لَا نَصْنَعُ إِلَيْهَا شَيْئًا مِنَ الْمَعْرُوفِ إِلَّا قَالَتْ: وَقَاكِ اللَّهُ عَذَابَ الْقَبْرِ. قَالَ: "كَذَبَتْ يَهُودُ . وَهُمْ عَلَى اللَّهِ أَكْذَبُ، لَا عَذَابَ دُونَ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ". ثُمَّ مَكَثَ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَمْكُثَ، فَخَرَجَ ذَاتَ يَوْمٍ نِصْفَ النَّهَارِ مُشْتَمِلًا بِثَوْبِهِ، مُحْمَرَّةً عَيْنَاهُ، وَهُوَ يُنَادِي بِأَعْلَى صَوْتِهِ: "الْقَبْرُ كَقِطَعِ اللَّيْلِ المظلمز أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، لَوْ تَعْلَمُونَ مَا أَعْلَمُ لَبَكَيْتُمْ كَثِيرًا وَضَحِكْتُمْ قَلِيلًا. أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، اسْتَعِيذُوا بِاللَّهِ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ، فَإِنَّ عَذَابَ الْقَبْرِ حَقٌّ" .

وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ عَلَى شَرْطِ الْبُخَارِيِّ وَمُسْلِمٍ، وَلَمْ يُخَرِّجَاهُ.

وَرَوَى أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ -قَالَ: سَأَلَتْهَا امْرَأَةٌ يَهُودِيَّةٌ فَأَعْطَتْهَا، فَقَالَتْ لَهَا: أَعَاذَكِ اللَّهُ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ. فَأَنْكَرَتْ عَائِشَةُ ذَلِكَ، فَلَمَّا رَأَتْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَتِ لَهُ، فَقَالَ: "لَا". قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: ثُمَّ قَالَ لَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ: "وَإِنَّهُ أُوحِيَ إلي أنكم تفتنون في قبوركم".

وَهَذَا أَيْضًا عَلَى شَرْطِهِمَا .

فَيُقَالُ: فَمَا الْجَمْعُ بَيْنَ هَذَا وَبَيْنَ كَوْنِ الْآيَةِ مَكِّيَّةً، وَفِيهَا الدَّلِيلُ عَلَى عَذَابِ الْبَرْزَخِ؟ وَالْجَوَابُ: أَنَّ الْآيَةَ دَلَّتْ عَلَى عَرْضِ الْأَرْوَاحِ إِلَى النَّارِ غُدُوًّا وَعَشِيًّا فِي الْبَرْزَخِ، وَلَيْسَ فِيهَا دَلَالَةٌ عَلَى اتِّصَالِ تَأَلُّمِهَا بِأَجْسَادِهَا فِي الْقُبُورِ، إِذْ قَدْ يَكُونُ ذَلِكَ مُخْتَصًّا بِالرُّوحِ، فَأَمَّا حُصُولُ ذَلِكَ لِلْجَسَدِ وَتَأَلُّمُهُ بِسَبَبِهِ، فَلَمْ يَدُلَّ عَلَيْهِ إِلَّا السُّنَّةُ فِي الْأَحَادِيثِ الْمَرْضِيَّةِ الْآتِي ذِكْرُهَا.

وَقَدْ يُقَالُ إِنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ إِنَّمَا دَلَّتْ عَلَى عَذَابِ الْكُفَّارِ فِي الْبَرْزَخِ، وَلَا يَلْزَمُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ أَنْ يُعَذَّبَ الْمُؤْمِنُ فِي قَبْرِهِ بِذَنْبٍ، وَمِمَّا يَدُلُّ عَلَى هَذَا مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا عُثْمَانُ بْنُ عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ دَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا وَعِنْدَهَا امْرَأَةٌ مِنَ الْيَهُودِ، وَهِيَ تَقُولُ: أَشَعَرْتِ أَنَّكُمْ تُفْتَنُونَ فِي قُبُورِكُمْ؟ فَارْتَاعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَقَالَ: "إِنَّمَا يُفْتَنُ يَهُودُ" قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: فَلَبِثْنَا لَيَالِيَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَشَعَرْتِ أَنَّهُ أُوحِيَ إِلَيَّ أَنَّكُمْ تُفْتَنُونَ فِي الْقُبُورِ؟ " وَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: سَمِعْتُ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم بعد يَسْتَعِيذُ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، عَنْ هَارُونَ بْنِ سَعِيدٍ وَحَرْمَلَةَ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنِ ابْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ يُونُسَ بْنِ يَزِيدَ الْأَيْلِيِّ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ .

وَقَدْ يُقَالُ: إِنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ دَلَّتْ عَلَى عَذَابِ الْأَرْوَاحِ فِي الْبَرْزَخِ، وَلَا يَلْزَمُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ أَنْ يَتَّصِلَ بِالْأَجْسَادِ فِي قُبُورِهَا، فَلَمَّا أُوحِيَ إِلَيْهِ فِي ذَلِكَ بِخُصُوصِيَّتِهِ اسْتَعَاذَ مِنْهُ، وَاللَّهُ، سُبْحَانَهُ وَتَعَالَى، أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الْبُخَارِيُّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ شُعْبَةَ، عَنْ أَشْعَثَ بْنِ أَبِي الشَّعْثَاءِ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، أَنَّ يَهُودِيَّةً دَخَلَتْ عَلَيْهَا فَقَالَتْ: أَعَاذَكِ اللَّهُ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ . فَسَأَلَتْ عَائِشَةُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ؟ فَقَالَ: "نَعَمْ عَذَابُ الْقَبْرِ حَقٌّ". قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: فَمَا رَأَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بعدُ صَلَّى صَلَاةً إِلَّا تَعَوَّذَ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ .

فَهَذَا يَدُلُّ عَلَى أَنَّهُ بَادَرَ إِلَى تَصْدِيقِ الْيَهُودِيَّةِ فِي هَذَا الْخَبَرِ، وَقَرَّرَ عَلَيْهِ. وَفِي الْأَخْبَارِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ: أَنَّهُ أَنْكَرَ ذَلِكَ حَتَّى جَاءَهُ الْوَحْيُ، فَلَعَلَّهُمَا قَضِيَّتَانِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، وَأَحَادِيثُ عَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿غُدُوًّا وَعَشِيًّا﴾ صَبَاحًا وَمَسَاءً، مَا بَقِيَتِ الدُّنْيَا، يُقَالُ لَهُمْ: يَا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ، هَذِهِ مَنَازِلُكُمْ، تَوْبِيخًا وَنِقْمَةً وصَغَارا لَهُمْ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ: هُمْ فِيهَا الْيَوْمَ يُغدَى بِهِمْ وَيُرَاحُ إلى أن تقوم الساعة.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُحَارِبِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا لَيْثٌ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ ثَرْوَانَ، عَنْ هُذَيْلٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: إِنَّ أَرْوَاحَ الشُّهَدَاءِ فِي أَجْوَافِ طَيْرٍ خُضْرٍ تَسْرَحُ بِهِمْ فِي الْجَنَّةِ حَيْثُ شَاءُوا، وَإِنَّ أَرْوَاحَ وِلْدَانِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي أَجْوَافِ عَصَافِيرَ تَسْرَحُ فِي الْجَنَّةِ حَيْثُ شَاءَتْ، فَتَأْوِي إِلَى قَنَادِيلَ مُعَلَّقَةٍ فِي الْعَرْشِ، وَإِنَّ أَرْوَاحَ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ فِي أَجْوَافِ طَيْرٍ سُودٍ تَغْدُو عَلَى جَهَنَّمَ وَتَرُوحُ عَلَيْهَا، فَذَلِكَ عَرْضُهَا.

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الثَّوْرِيُّ عَنْ أبي قيس عن الهُزَيل ابن شُرَحْبِيلَ، مِنْ كَلَامِهِ فِي أَرْوَاحِ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ.

وَفِي حَدِيثِ الْإِسْرَاءِ مِنْ رِوَايَةِ أَبِي هَارُونَ الْعَبْدِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ فِيهِ: "ثُمَّ انْطُلِقَ بِي إِلَى خَلْقٍ كَثِيرٍ مِنْ خَلْقِ اللَّهِ، رجالٌ كلُّ رَجُلٍ مِنْهُمْ بَطْنُهُ مِثْلُ الْبَيْتِ الضَّخْمِ، مُصَفَّدُونَ عَلَى سَابِلَةِ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَآلُ فِرْعَوْنَ يُعْرَضُونَ عَلَى النَّارِ غُدُوًّا وَعَشِيًّا. ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ أَدْخِلُوا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ أَشَدَّ الْعَذَابِ﴾ وَآلُ فِرْعَوْنَ كَالْإِبِلِ الْمُسَوَّمَةِ يَخْبِطُونَ الْحِجَارَةَ وَالشَّجَرَ وَلَا يَعْقِلُونَ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ أخْرَم، حَدَّثَنَا عَامِرُ بْنُ مُدْرِك الْحَارِثِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عُتْبَةُ -يَعْنِي ابْنَ يَقْظَانَ-عَنْ قَيْسِ بْنِ مسلم، عن طارق، عن شِهَابٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا أَحْسَنَ مُحْسِنٌ مِنْ مُسْلِمٍ أَوْ كَافِرٍ إِلَّا أَثَابَهُ اللَّهُ". قَالَ: قُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ مَا إِثَابَةُ الْكَافِرِ؟ فَقَالَ: "إِنْ كَانَ قَدْ وَصَلَ رَحِمًا أَوْ تَصَدَّقَ بِصَدَقَةٍ أَوْ عَمِلَ حَسَنَةً، أَثَابَهُ اللَّهُ الْمَالَ وَالْوَلَدَ وَالصِّحَّةَ وَأَشْبَاهَ ذَلِكَ". قُلْنَا: فَمَا إِثَابَتُهُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ؟ قَالَ: "عَذَابًا دُونَ الْعَذَابِ" وَقَرَأَ: ﴿أَدْخِلُوا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ أَشَدَّ الْعَذَابِ﴾ وَرَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مَسْنَدِهِ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أخْرَم، ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَا نَعْلَمُ لَهُ إِسْنَادًا غَيْرَ هَذَا .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْكَرِيمِ بْنُ أَبِي عُمَيْرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الْفَزَارِيُّ الْبَلْخِيُّ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ الْأَوْزَاعِيَّ وَسَأَلَهُ رَجُلٌ فَقَالَ: رَحِمَكَ اللَّهُ. رَأَيْنَا طُيُورًا تَخْرُجُ مِنَ الْبَحْرِ، تَأْخُذُ نَاحِيَةَ الْغَرْبِ بِيضًا، فَوْجًا فَوْجًا، لَا يَعْلَمُ عَدَدَهَا إِلَّا اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَإِذَا كَانَ الْعَشِيُّ رَجَعَ مِثْلُهَا سُودًا. قَالَ: وَفَطِنْتُمْ إِلَى ذَلِكَ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: إِنَّ تِلْكَ الطَّيْرَ فِي حَوَاصِلِهَا أَرْوَاحُ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ، تُعْرَضُ عَلَى النَّارِ غُدُوًّا وَعَشِيًّا، فَتَرْجِعُ إِلَى وُكُورِهَا وَقَدِ احْتَرَقَتْ ريَاشُها وَصَارَتْ سُودًا، فَيَنْبُتُ عَلَيْهَا مِنَ اللَّيْلِ رِيشٌ أَبْيَضُ، وَيَتَنَاثَرُ السُّودُ، ثُمَّ تَغْدُو عَلَى النَّارِ غُدُوًّا وَعَشِيًّا، ثُمَّ تَرْجِعُ إِلَى وُكُورِهَا. فَذَلِكَ دَأْبُهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ الْقِيَامَةِ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَدْخِلُوا آلَ فِرْعَوْنَ أَشَدَّ الْعَذَابِ﴾ قَالَ: وكانوا يَقُولُونَ إِنَّهُمْ سِتُّمِائَةِ أَلْفِ مُقَاتِلٍ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا إِسْحَاقُ، أَخْبَرَنَا مَالِكٌ، عَنْ نَافِعٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ إِذَا مَاتَ عُرِضَ عَلَيْهِ مَقْعَدُهُ بِالْغَدَاةِ وَالْعَشِيِّ، إِنْ كَانَ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ فَمِنْ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ، وَإِنْ كَانَ مِنْ أَهْلِ النَّارِ فَمِنْ أَهْلِ النَّارِ. فَيُقَالُ: هَذَا مَقْعَدُكَ حَتَّى يَبْعَثَكَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَالِكٍ، بِهِ .

---

## 40:47-50 — verses 47-50 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about the mutual disputation of the people of the Fire within the Fire, and their contention with one another, and Pharaoh and his people are among them. {So the weak will say}, that is, the followers, {to those who were arrogant}, that is, the leaders, chiefs, and great ones: {Indeed, we were followers to you}, meaning, we obeyed you in what you called us to in the worldly life, of disbelief and misguidance, {so will you avert from us a portion of the Fire?}, that is, a share that you would bear on our behalf.

{Those who were arrogant will say, Indeed, all of us are in it}, meaning, we will not bear anything on your behalf; what we ourselves have of torment and punishment is enough for us. {Indeed, Allah has already judged between the servants}, meaning, He apportions the punishment among us according to what each of us deserves, as the Almighty said: {He will say, For each is double, but you do not know} [al-A'raf: 38].

{And those in the Fire will say to the keepers of Hell, Call upon your Lord to lighten for us a day of the punishment}. When they knew that Allah, glorified is He, would not respond to them nor listen to their supplication, and had indeed said: {Remain in it despised, and do not speak to Me} [al-Mu'minun: 108], they asked the keepers, who are like gatekeepers for the people of the Fire, to call upon Allah for them, that He might lighten the punishment for the disbelievers even for a single day. The keepers said to them in rebuttal: {Did there not come to you your messengers with clear proofs?}, meaning, were the proofs not established against you in the worldly life through the tongues of the messengers? {They will say, Yes indeed. They will say, Then call yourselves}, that is, you call for yourselves, for we will not call on your behalf, nor listen to you, nor wish for your deliverance; we are free of you. Then we inform you that whether you call or do not call, you will not be answered, nor will anything be lightened for you. Therefore they said: {And the supplication of the disbelievers is not except in error}, meaning, except in futility, neither accepted nor answered.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ تَحَاجِّ أَهْلِ النَّارِ فِي النَّارِ، وَتَخَاصُمِهِمْ، وَفِرْعَوْنُ وَقَوْمُهُ مَنْ جُمْلَتِهِمْ ﴿فَيَقُولُ الضُّعَفَاءُ﴾ وَهُمُ: الْأَتْبَاعُ ﴿لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا﴾ وَهُمُ: الْقَادَةُ وَالسَّادَةُ وَالْكُبَرَاءُ: ﴿إِنَّا كُنَّا لَكُمْ تَبَعًا﴾ أَيْ: أَطَعْنَاكُمْ فِيمَا دَعَوْتُمُونَا إِلَيْهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَالضَّلَالِ، ﴿فَهَلْ أَنْتُمْ مُغْنُونَ عَنَّا نَصِيبًا مِنَ النَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: قِسْطًا تَتَحَمَّلُونَهُ عَنَّا.

﴿قَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا إِنَّا كُلٌّ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: لَا نَتَحَمَّلُ عَنْكُمْ شَيْئًا، كَفَى بِنَا مَا عِنْدَنَا، وَمَا حَمَلْنَا مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالنَّكَالِ. ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ حَكَمَ بَيْنَ الْعِبَادِ﴾ أَيْ: يَقْسِمُ بَيْنَنَا الْعَذَابَ بِقَدْرِ مَا يَسْتَحِقُّهُ كُلٌّ مِنَّا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالَ لِكُلٍّ ضِعْفٌ وَلَكِنْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٣٨] .

﴿وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ فِي النَّارِ لِخَزَنَةِ جَهَنَّمَ ادْعُوا رَبَّكُمْ يُخَفِّفْ عَنَّا يَوْمًا مِنَ الْعَذَابِ﴾ لَمَّا عَلِمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ، سُبْحَانَهُ، لَا يَسْتَجِيبُ مِنْهُمْ وَلَا يَسْتَمِعُ لِدُعَائِهِمْ، بَلْ قَدْ قال: ﴿اخْسَؤُوا فِيهَا وَلا تُكَلِّمُونِ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ:١٠٨] سَأَلُوا الْخَزَنَةَ -وَهُمْ كَالْبَوَّابِينَ لِأَهْلِ النَّارِ-أَنْ يَدْعُوا لَهُمُ اللَّهَ أَنْ يُخَفِّفَ عَنِ الْكَافِرِينَ وَلَوْ يَوْمًا وَاحِدًا مِنَ الْعَذَابِ، فَقَالَتْ لَهُمُ الْخَزَنَةُ رَادِّينَ عَلَيْهِمْ:: ﴿أَوَ لَمْ تَكُ تَأْتِيكُمْ رُسُلُكُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: أَوَمَا قَامَتْ عَلَيْكُمُ الْحُجَجُ فِي الدُّنْيَا عَلَى أَلْسِنَةِ الرُّسُلِ؟ ﴿قَالُوا بَلَى قَالُوا فَادْعُوا﴾ أَيْ: أَنْتُمْ لِأَنْفُسِكُمْ، فَنَحْنُ لَا نَدْعُو لَكُمْ وَلَا نَسْمَعُ مِنْكُمْ وَلَا نَوَدُّ خَلَاصَكُمْ، وَنَحْنُ مِنْكُمْ بَرَآءُ، ثُمَّ نُخْبِرُكُمْ أَنَّهُ سَوَاءٌ دَعَوْتُمْ أَوْ لَمْ تَدْعُوا لَا يُسْتَجَابُ لَكُمْ وَلَا يُخَفَّفُ عَنْكُمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا : ﴿وَمَا دُعَاءُ الْكَافِرِينَ إِلا فِي ضَلالٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِلَّا مِنْ ذَهَابٍ، لَا يُتَقَبَّلُ وَلَا يستجاب.

---

## 40:51-56 — verses 51-56 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir, may God Almighty have mercy on him, raised a question regarding the words of the Almighty: {Indeed We shall surely aid Our messengers and those who believe, in the life of this world}. He said: it is known that some of the prophets, upon them be prayer and peace, were killed outright by their people, such as Yahya, Zakariyya, and Sha'ya (Isaiah). Among them were some who departed from among their people, either as emigrants like Ibrahim (peace be upon him), or by being raised to heaven like Isa (peace be upon him). So where is the aid in this world?

He then answered this with two answers.

The first: that the report is expressed in general terms while what is meant is only some of them. He said: this is permissible in the language.

The second: that what is meant by aid is retribution taken on their behalf against those who harmed them, whether this occurred in their presence, in their absence, or after their death, just as was done to the killers of Yahya, Zakariyya, and Sha'ya. Enemies were given power over those killers who humiliated them and shed their blood. It has been mentioned that God seized Nimrod with the seizing of One mighty and able. As for those among the Jews who sought to crucify the Messiah (peace be upon him), God gave the Romans power over them, and they humiliated them and abased them, and God made the Romans triumphant over them. Then, before the Day of Resurrection, Isa son of Maryam will descend as a just leader and equitable judge. He will kill the Dajjal (the Antichrist, the deceiving false messiah) and his soldiers from among the Jews, kill the swine, break the cross, and abolish the jizya (poll tax), accepting nothing but Islam. This is a mighty aid. This is the way of God among His creation, in ancient times and in recent times: that He aids His believing servants in this world and cools their eyes by dealing with those who harmed them. In Sahih al-Bukhari, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, he said: "God Almighty says: whoever shows enmity to a friend of Mine, I declare war upon him." And in another hadith: "I truly take vengeance for My friends as the fierce lion takes vengeance." For this reason, the Almighty destroyed the people of Nuh, 'Ad, Thamud, the people of al-Rass, the people of Lut, the people of Madyan, and their likes and counterparts among those who denied the messengers and opposed the truth. God rescued the believers from among them, destroying none of them, while He punished the disbelievers, letting none of them escape.

Al-Suddi said: God never sent a messenger to a people who then killed him, nor a group of believers who called to the truth and were then killed, without that generation passing away only for God to raise up for them one who would aid them, seeking their blood from those who had done that to them, in this world. He said: thus the prophets and believers were killed in this world, yet they were aided within it.

Thus did God, [glory be to Him], aid His Prophet Muhammad ﷺ and his companions over those who opposed him, contended with him, denied him, and showed him enmity. He made His word the highest, and His religion manifest over all other religions. He commanded him to emigrate from among his people to the Prophetic City (Madinah), and appointed for him there helpers and supporters. Then He granted him the necks of the polytheists on the Day of Badr, giving him victory over them and abandoning them before him. He killed their chieftains and captured their nobles, driving them off bound together in chains, then showed them favor by taking ransom from them. Then, after a short period, He opened Makkah for him, and his eye was cooled by his own city, the sacred, forbidden, honored, and exalted city. Through it God rescued him from the polytheism and disbelief he had been surrounded by, and opened Yemen for him, and the whole Arabian Peninsula submitted to him, and people entered the religion of God in multitudes. Then God, the Exalted, took him unto Himself, on account of the immense honor he held with Him, and God established his companions as successors after him. They conveyed from him the religion of God and called God's servants to God. They conquered lands, districts, provinces, cities, and towns, and won hearts, until the Muhammadan call spread to the easts and wests of the earth. This religion continues to stand, aided and manifest, until the establishment of the Hour. For this reason the Almighty said: {Indeed We shall surely aid Our messengers and those who believe, in the life of this world and on the Day when the witnesses will stand}, meaning: on the Day of Resurrection the aid will be greater, mightier, and more magnificent.

Mujahid said: the witnesses are the angels.

His statement: {The Day when the excuse of the wrongdoers will not benefit them} is a substitution for His statement {and on the Day when the witnesses will stand}.

Others read "yawmu" in the nominative case, as though he were explaining it thereby: {and on the Day when the witnesses will stand, the Day when the excuse will not benefit the wrongdoers}, meaning the polytheists, {their excuse}, that is, no excuse or ransom will be accepted from them, {and theirs is the curse}, that is, banishment and expulsion from mercy, {and theirs is the evil abode}, which is the Fire. This is what al-Suddi said: what an evil dwelling and resting place.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas: {and theirs is the evil abode} meaning: an evil outcome.

His statement: {And We certainly gave Musa guidance}, that is, the guidance and light with which God sent him, {and We caused the Children of Israel to inherit the Book}, meaning: We made the final outcome theirs, and We caused them to inherit the lands of Pharaoh, his wealth, his stores, and his land, because of their patient endurance in obedience to God and following His messenger Musa (peace be upon him). And in the Book which they were caused to inherit, that is the Torah, there is {guidance and reminder for people of understanding}, meaning: sound and sensible minds.

His statement: {So be patient}, that is, O Muhammad, {indeed the promise of God is true}, meaning: We promised you that We would raise your word high and make the final outcome yours and that of those who follow you, and God does not break His promise. This which We have informed you of is truth, in which there is no doubt or uncertainty.

His statement: {And seek forgiveness for your sin}, this is an incitement for the community to seek forgiveness. {And glorify with the praise of your Lord in the evening}, meaning: in the latter part of the day and the early part of the night, {and in the morning}, that is, the early part of the day and the latter part of the night.

His statement: {Indeed, those who dispute concerning the signs of God without any authority having come to them}, meaning: they repel truth with falsehood, and reject sound proofs with corrupt doubts, without any evidence or proof from God. {There is nothing in their breasts but pride, which they will never attain}, meaning: there is nothing in their breasts except arrogance against following the truth, and contempt for the one who brought it to them, and what they seek in suppressing the truth and elevating falsehood will never be achieved for them. Rather, the truth is what shall be raised, and their word and aim is what shall be laid low. {So seek refuge in God}, that is, from the condition of the likes of these people, {indeed He is the Hearing, the Seeing}, or from the evil of the likes of these disputers regarding the signs of God without authority. This is the interpretation of Ibn Jarir.

Ka'b and Abu al-'Aliyah said: this verse was revealed concerning the Jews: {Indeed, those who dispute concerning the signs of God without any authority having come to them, there is nothing in their breasts but pride, which they will never attain}. Abu al-'Aliyah said: this is because they claimed that the Dajjal was one of them, and that through him they would possess the earth. So God said to His Prophet ﷺ, commanding him to seek refuge from the trial of the Dajjal. For this reason He said: {So seek refuge in God, indeed He is the Hearing, the Seeing}.

This is a gharib (strange) statement, and it involves a far-fetched forcing of the text, although Ibn Abi Hatim did narrate it in his book. And God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَدْ أَوْرَدَ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، عِنْدَ قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّا لَنَنْصُرُ رُسُلَنَا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا﴾ سُؤَالًا فَقَالَ: قَدْ عُلِم أَنَّ بَعْضَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، عَلَيْهِمُ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، قَتَلَهُ قَوْمُهُ بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ كَيَحْيَى وَزَكَرِيَّا وَشَعْيَاءَ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ خَرَجَ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَظْهُرِهِمْ إِمَّا مُهَاجِرًا كَإِبْرَاهِيمَ ، وَإِمَّا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ كَعِيسَى ، فَأَيْنَ النُّصْرَةُ فِي الدُّنْيَا؟ ثُمَّ أَجَابَ عَنْ ذَلِكَ بِجَوَابَيْنِ .

أَحَدُهُمَا: أَنْ يَكُونَ الْخَبَرُ خَرَجَ عَامًّا، وَالْمُرَادُ بِهِ الْبَعْضُ، قَالَ: وَهَذَا سَائِغٌ فِي اللُّغَةِ.

الثَّانِي: أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ بِالنَّصْرِ الِانْتِصَارُ لَهُمْ مِمَّنْ آذَاهُمْ، وَسَوَاءٌ كَانَ ذَلِكَ بِحَضْرَتِهِمْ أَوْ فِي غَيْبَتِهِمْ أَوْ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهِمْ، كَمَا فُعِلَ بِقَتَلَةِ يَحْيَى وَزَكَرِيَّا وَشَعْيَاءَ، سُلِّطَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ أَعْدَائِهِمْ مَنْ أَهَانَهُمْ وَسَفَكَ دِمَاءَهُمْ، وَقَدْ ذُكِرَ أَنَّ النُّمْرُوذَ أَخَذَهُ اللَّهُ أَخْذَ عَزِيزٍ مُقْتَدِرٍ، وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ رَامُوا صَلْبَ الْمَسِيحِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مِنَ الْيَهُودِ، فَسَلَّطَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمُ الرُّومَ فَأَهَانُوهُمْ وَأَذَلُّوهُمْ، وَأَظْهَرَهُمُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ. ثُمَّ قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ سَيَنْزِلُ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ إِمَامًا عَادِلًا وَحَكَمًا مُقْسِطًا، فَيَقْتُلُ الْمَسِيحَ الدَّجَّالَ وَجُنُودَهُ مِنَ الْيَهُودِ، وَيَقْتُلُ الْخِنْزِيرَ، وَيَكْسِرُ الصَّلِيبَ، وَيَضَعُ الْجِزْيَةَ فَلَا يَقْبَلُ إِلَّا الْإِسْلَامَ. وَهَذِهِ نُصْرَةٌ عَظِيمَةٌ، وَهَذِهِ سُنَّةُ اللَّهِ فِي خَلْقِهِ فِي قَدِيمِ الدَّهْرِ وَحَدِيثِهِ: أَنَّهُ يَنْصُرُ عِبَادَهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَيُقِرُّ أَعْيُنَهُمْ مِمَّنْ آذَاهُمْ، فَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: مَنْ عَادَى لِي وَلِيًّا فَقَدْ بَارَزَنِي بِالْحَرْبِ" وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "إِنِّي لِأَثْأَرُ لِأَوْلِيَائِي كَمَا يَثْأَرُ اللَّيْثُ الْحِرِبُ" ؛ وَلِهَذَا أَهْلَكَ تَعَالَى قَوْمَ نُوحٍ وَعَادٍ وَثَمُودَ، وَأَصْحَابَ الرَّسِّ، وَقَوْمَ لُوطٍ، وَأَهْلَ مَدْيَنَ، وَأَشْبَاهَهُمْ وَأَضْرَابَهُمْ مِمَّنْ كَذَّبَ الرُّسُلَ وَخَالَفَ الْحَقَّ. وَأَنْجَى اللَّهُ مِنْ بَيْنِهِمُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَلَمْ يُهْلِكْ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدًا وَعَذَّبَ الْكَافِرِينَ، فَلَمْ يُفْلِتْ مِنْهُمْ أَحَدًا .

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: لَمْ يَبْعَثِ اللَّهُ رَسُولًا قَطُّ إِلَى قَوْمٍ فَيَقْتُلُونَهُ، أَوْ قَوْمًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ يَدْعُونَ إِلَى الْحَقِّ فَيُقْتَلُونَ، فَيَذْهَبُ ذَلِكَ الْقَرْنُ حَتَّى يَبْعَثَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ مَنْ يَنْصُرُهُمْ، فَيَطْلُبُ بِدِمَائِهِمْ مِمَّنْ فَعَلَ ذَلِكَ بِهِمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا. قَالَ: فَكَانَتِ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ يُقْتَلُونَ فِي الدنيا، وهم منصورون فيها.

وَهَكَذَا نَصَرَ اللَّهُ [سُبْحَانَهُ] نَبِيَّهُ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ وَأَصْحَابَهُ عَلَى مَنْ خَالَفَهُ وَنَاوَأَهُ، وَكَذَّبَهُ وَعَادَاهُ، فَجَعَلَ كَلِمَتَهُ هِيَ الْعُلْيَا، وَدِينَهُ هُوَ الظَّاهِرَ عَلَى سَائِرِ الْأَدْيَانِ. وَأَمَرَهُ بِالْهِجْرَةِ مِنْ بَيْنِ ظَهْرَانَيْ قَوْمِهِ إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ النَّبَوِيَّةِ، وَجَعَلَ لَهُ فِيهَا أَنْصَارًا وَأَعْوَانًا، ثُمَّ مَنَحَهُ أَكْتَافَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ يَوْمَ بَدْرٍ، فَنَصْرَهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَخَذَلَهُمْ لَهُ، وَقَتَلَ صَنَادِيدَهُمْ، وَأَسَرَ سَرَاتَهُمْ، فَاسْتَاقَهُمْ مُقَرَّنِينَ فِي الْأَصْفَادِ، ثُمَّ مَنَّ عَلَيْهِمْ بِأَخْذِهِ الْفِدَاءَ مِنْهُمْ، ثُمَّ بَعْدَ مُدَّةٍ قَرِيبَةٍ فَتَحَ [عَلَيْهِ] مَكَّةَ، فَقَرَّتْ عَيْنُهُ بِبَلَدِهِ، وَهُوَ الْبَلَدُ الْمُحَرَّمُ الْحَرَامُ الْمُشَرَّفُ الْمُعَظَّمُ، فَأَنْقَذَهُ اللَّهُ بِهِ مِمَّا كَانَ فِيهِ مِنَ الشِّرْكِ وَالْكُفْرِ، وَفَتَحَ لَهُ الْيَمَنَ، وَدَانَتْ لَهُ جَزِيرَةُ الْعَرَبِ بِكَمَالِهَا، وَدَخَلَ النَّاسُ فِي دِينِ اللَّهِ أَفْوَاجًا. ثُمَّ قَبَضَهُ اللَّهُ، تَعَالَى، إِلَيْهِ لِمَا لَهُ عِنْدَهُ مِنَ الْكَرَامَةِ الْعَظِيمَةِ، فَأَقَامَ اللَّهُ أَصْحَابَهُ خُلَفَاءَ بَعْدَهُ، فَبَلَّغُوا عَنْهُ دِينَ اللَّهِ، وَدَعَوْا عِبَادَ اللَّهِ إِلَى اللَّهِ. وَفَتَحُوا الْبِلَادَ وَالرَّسَاتِيقَ وَالْأَقَالِيمَ وَالْمَدَائِنَ وَالْقُرَى وَالْقُلُوبَ، حَتَّى انْتَشَرَتِ الدَّعْوَةُ الْمُحَمَّدِيَّةُ فِي مَشَارِقِ الْأَرْضِ وَمَغَارِبِهَا. ثُمَّ لَا يَزَالُ هَذَا الدِّينُ قَائِمًا مَنْصُورًا ظَاهِرًا إِلَى قِيَامِ السَّاعَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّا لَنَنْصُرُ رُسُلَنَا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَيَوْمَ يَقُومُ الأشْهَادُ﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ تَكُونُ النُّصْرَةُ أَعْظَمَ وَأَكْبَرَ وَأَجَلَّ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْأَشْهَادُ: الْمَلَائِكَةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَوْمَ لَا يَنْفَعُ الظَّالِمِينَ مَعْذِرَتُهُمْ﴾ بَدَلٌ مِنْ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَيَوْمَ يَقُومُ الأشْهَادُ﴾ .

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: "يَوْمُ" بِالرَّفْعِ، كَأَنَّهُ فَسَّرَهُ بِهِ ﴿وَيَوْمَ يَقُومُ الأشْهَادُ يَوْمَ لَا يَنْفَعُ الظَّالِمِين﴾ ، وَهُمُ الْمُشْرِكُونَ ﴿مَعْذِرَتُهُم﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُقْبَلُ مِنْهُمْ عُذْرٌ وَلَا فِدْيَةٌ، ﴿وَلَهُمُ اللَّعْنَةُ﴾ أَيِ: الْإِبْعَادُ وَالطَّرْدُ مِنَ الرَّحْمَةِ، ﴿وَلَهُمْ سُوءُ الدَّارِ﴾ وَهِيَ النَّارُ. قَالَهُ السُّدِّيُّ، بِئْسَ الْمَنْزِلُ وَالْمَقِيلُ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ سُوءُ الدَّارِ﴾ أَيْ: سُوءُ الْعَاقِبَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا مُوسَى الْهُدَى﴾ وَهُوَ مَا بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ بِهِ مِنَ الْهُدَى وَالنُّورِ، ﴿وَأَوْرَثْنَا بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ الْكِتَابَ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلْنَا لَهُمُ الْعَاقِبَةَ، وَأَوْرَثْنَاهُمْ بِلَادَ فِرْعَوْنَ وَأَمْوَالَهُ وَحَوَاصِلَهُ وَأَرْضَهُ، بِمَا صَبَرُوا عَلَى طَاعَةِ اللَّهِ وَاتِّبَاعِ رَسُولِهِ مُوسَى، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَفِي الْكِتَابِ الَّذِي أُورِثُوهُ -وَهُوَ التَّوْرَاةُ- ﴿هُدًى وَذِكْرَى لأولِي الألْبَابِ﴾ وَهِيَ: الْعُقُولُ الصَّحِيحَةُ السَّلِيمَةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَاصْبِرْ﴾ أَيْ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ﴿إِنَّ وَعْدَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: وَعَدْنَاكَ أَنَّا سَنُعْلِي كَلِمَتَكَ، وَنَجْعَلُ الْعَاقِبَةَ لَكَ وَلِمَنِ اتَّبَعَكَ، وَاللَّهُ لَا يُخْلِفُ الْمِيعَادَ. وَهَذَا الَّذِي أَخْبَرْنَاكَ بِهِ حَقٌّ لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ وَلَا شَكَّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاسْتَغْفِرْ لِذَنْبِكَ﴾ هَذَا تَهْيِيجٌ لِلْأُمَّةِ عَلَى الِاسْتِغْفَارِ، ﴿وَسَبِّحْ بِحَمْدِ رَبِّكَ بِالْعَشِيِّ﴾ أَيْ: فِي أَوَاخِرِ النَّهَارِ وَأَوَائِلِ اللَّيْلِ، ﴿وَالإبْكَارِ﴾ وَهِيَ أَوَائِلُ النَّهَارِ وَأَوَاخِرُ اللَّيْلِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يُجَادِلُونَ فِي آيَاتِ اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ سُلْطَانٍ أَتَاهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يَدْفَعُونَ الْحَقَّ بِالْبَاطِلِ، وَيَرُدُّونَ الْحُجَجَ الصَّحِيحَةَ بِالشُّبَهِ الْفَاسِدَةِ بِلَا بُرْهَانٍ وَلَا حُجَّةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ، ﴿إِنْ فِي صُدُورِهِمْ إِلا كِبْرٌ مَا هُمْ بِبَالِغِيهِ﴾

أَيْ: مَا فِي صُدُورِهِمْ إِلَّا كِبَرٌ عَلَى اتِّبَاعِ الْحَقِّ، وَاحْتِقَارٌ لِمَنْ جَاءَهُمْ بِهِ، وَلَيْسَ مَا يَرُومُونَهُ مِنْ إِخْمَالِ الْحَقِّ وَإِعْلَاءِ الْبَاطِلِ بِحَاصِلٍ لَهُمْ، بَلِ الْحَقُّ هُوَ الْمَرْفُوعُ، وَقَوْلُهُمْ وَقَصْدُهُمْ هُوَ الْمَوْضُوعُ، ﴿فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ حَالِ مِثْلِ هَؤُلَاءِ، ﴿إِنَّه هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْبَصِيرُ﴾ أَوْ مِنْ شَرِّ مِثْلِ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُجَادِلِينَ فِي آيَاتِ اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ سُلْطَانٍ. هَذَا تَفْسِيرُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ كَعْبٌ وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي الْيَهُودِ: ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يُجَادِلُونَ فِي آيَاتِ اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ سُلْطَانٍ أَتَاهُمْ إِنْ فِي صُدُورِهِمْ إِلا كِبْرٌ مَا هُمْ بِبَالِغِيهِ﴾ قَالَ أَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ: وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمُ ادَّعَوْا أَنَّ الدَّجَّالَ مِنْهُمْ، وَأَنَّهُمْ يَمْلِكُونَ بِهِ الْأَرْضَ. فَقَالَ اللَّهُ لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ آمِرًا لَهُ أَنْ يَسْتَعِيذَ مِنْ فِتْنَةِ الدَّجَّالِ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَاسْتَعِذْ بِاللَّهِ إِنَّهُ هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْبَصِيرُ﴾ .

وَهَذَا قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَفِيهِ تَعَسُّفٌ بَعِيدٌ، وَإِنْ كَانَ قَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ فِي كِتَابِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 40:57-59 — verses 57-59 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says, calling attention to the fact that He will bring back creation on the Day of Resurrection, and that this is easy and simple for Him, by pointing out that He created the heavens and the earth, and that the creation of these two is greater than the creation of mankind, both in its origination and its repetition. So whoever is capable of that is capable, with even greater right and more fitting reason, of what is less than it. As the Exalted said: {Do they not see that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth and did not tire from creating them, is able to give life to the dead? Yes indeed, He is over all things Powerful} [al-Ahqaf: 33]. And here He says: {The creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of mankind, but most of mankind do not know}. This is why they do not reflect on this proof nor ponder it, just as many of the Arabs used to acknowledge that Allah created the heavens and the earth, yet denied the return to life, out of considering it far-fetched, out of disbelief, and out of stubbornness. They had acknowledged something more deserving of acceptance than what they denied.

Then He said: {And the blind and the seeing are not equal, nor are those who believe and do righteous deeds and the evildoer}, meaning: just as the blind person who sees nothing at all is not equal to the sighted person who sees whatever his sight reaches, rather there is a great difference between them, likewise the righteous believers and the sinful disbelievers are not equal. {Little do you reflect}, meaning: how little do most people take heed.

Then He said: {Indeed the Hour is coming}, meaning it is certain and will occur, {there is no doubt about it, but most of mankind do not believe}, meaning they do not affirm it as true, rather they deny that it will occur at all.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] an old shaykh from the people of Yemen, who had come from there, said: I heard that when the Hour draws near, tribulation upon mankind will intensify, and the heat of the sun will intensify.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this
